                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Direction of Providence  
<Summary of Words> The universe possesses a perfect and flawless ideal, which is the content of goodness. Goodness belongs to the Creator. There must be a historical heart to face the heart of heaven and earth. Today's world is a dreamlike world compared to thousands of years ago. The spirit world is the substantial world where the heart is expressed. For the heart to be joyful, the body must manifest as the counterpart of the heart.  
God created humans to align the heart, circumstances, and desires. However, humans fell without knowing God's heart, circumstances, and desires. Nevertheless, God established humans to guide the direction of history. God has sought a historical faith nation.  
Jesus came to establish a worldwide faith-centered principle. Faith, from the perspective of God's sovereignty, transcends the dimensions of the world. It is a noun that cannot be expressed at the level of nations. Thus, Jesus must come again. The view of faith regarding heaven and earth refers to what aligns with God's heart, circumstances, and desires.  
Someone who knows God's heart, circumstances, and desires must emerge. An ideology and view of faith centered on God's heart, circumstances, and desires must arise. Those responsible for religion cannot be swayed by any ideology.  
Creation begins with establishing the core first. The external must align with the internal.  
External and internal must be combined.  
Offerings are classified into external offerings and internal offerings. Cain is external, and Abel is internal. Noah's internal position was determined after undergoing the external judgment of 40 days. Jacob's internal position was also determined after the external journey of 21 years. Providence is the same from small to large.  
When God drove the Israelite nation out of Egypt, He hardened Pharaoh's heart. Whenever God carries out a new providence, He strikes to restore. Therefore, it is wise to prepare in advance for a new providence.  
Moses died because he could not drive out the Israelite nation. The three-year period was like establishing a standard for liberating the Israelite nation before Pharaoh while enduring unspeakable hardships.  
The 72 families represent the Cain and Abel type. It is horizontal.  
When one place is established, another place collapses. Therefore, the communist world will crumble.  
Past ancestors could not fulfill their responsibilities, but you must not forget that you are also people who have not fulfilled your responsibilities. You must know that your life is the life of the nation, state, and history.  

2)  
The Path of Unification Church Members  
<Summary of Words> Even if sovereignty collapses, we must become a nation that leaves behind a culture capable of governing future generations.  
History judges the era, and the era judges history. The 6,000 years of tears must manifest as reality.  
The teacher practiced before speaking. I can confidently say that he is better than any loyal subject or hero from any past era. He has confidence.  
A personal textbook is needed. There must be someone who can say that anyone should be like me.  
Jesus had to organize Judaism and the Israelite nation. And the Israelite nation had to submit to the organized Judaism. Similarly, the world must submit to the ideology of religion.  
The first operation has succeeded. What we have done in the Unification Church is something no one else can do.  
Jesus sought God hidden in the Pentateuch. You must become those who relieve Jesus' resentment. You must become Jesus' relatives and siblings. Jesus first called his brothers. Because Jesus did not have family and household, he could not have a tribe and sovereignty.  
After the 124 couples' blessing ceremony, a dedication ceremony was held. The one who must come as a resurrected being to establish a personal, familial, tribal, and national foundation is the Lord of the Second Advent. He worked for three years. This three-year period corresponds to the period of finding children (the tribal period). This period is when, just as Jesus had to organize Judaism and the Israelite nation, a resurrected being is established, and similar work is done.  
Historical figures from the past, such as Noah, Abraham, and Moses, were ignorant people.  
You must subjugate three generations to become God's sons and daughters. God must also stand in the position of ancestors before Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent. Noah sent out the dove three times before coming down from the ark.  
The teacher must resolve the deep-seated resentment across the three generations of Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent. During this three-year period, 36, 72, and 124 families must be blessed. Thus, a global standard must be established through three stages.  
Humans fell by losing faith, heart, and substance.  
The teacher sought to find the person who would be most faithful to God, who would speak the most unbelievable words.  
He tested those who said, "I am the wife of Jehovah," or "I am the Lord," to see if they had faith that could replace history, a heart, and substance.  
After determining faith, he proclaimed the resurrection of the heart and substance. After establishing what came vertically, he blessed it horizontally.  
He awarded based on this standard. After establishing this horizontal standard, he selected holy sites, and this offering is the dedication ceremony. Through this dedication ceremony, what is vertical was developed horizontally, and a flat standard was established. Therefore, since August, the world has been moving in a different direction, and conflicts are occurring even in the communist world.  
This era is to create living materials. For the next four years, we must act under the slogan of becoming victorious subjects. We have endured well, so now let us take the offensive.  
Now we must restore all things. I am trying to make you living textbooks. The era of church missions has passed, and the struggle that involves the nation will begin. After passing through the era centered on individuals, the era centered on families will come, so we must establish a nation centered on heaven.  
You must know that there is no path for this nation other than the path of Unification Church members. We must implement a movement to save one won daily.  
For the tribe to rest, the nation must rest. Therefore, we must endure tribal hardships.  
The last year of the four-year course will be the 21st year since the start of the mission for the purpose (calculated from the age of 26 when the Pyongyang evangelism began).  
Now the Unification Church is establishing a national standard, so it cannot hold onto individuals. Therefore, if individuals lose their strength, they must regain their strength.  
You must know how to serve three generations and lead three generations. You must not report horizontally regarding the person you should serve. Up to three generations above can be reported freely.  

3)  
Holy Sites and Holy Objects to Be Found  
<Summary of Words> You must become someone who can keep God's will and leave it behind, and someone who can dedicate all things to the holy land.  
Blessed families must establish God's things on the foundation that realizes the eternal creation ideal that God desires.  
Through us, God can sing of the ideal world of goodness, that is, the garden of the heart. But can you view the world of the heart as the owners of the holy land that God desires?  
You must love the three thousand li as a condition for the holy land. You must want to live on this land and sweat on this land. You must know that there is a tradition of bloody history on this land and remember the Father.  
Receiving a blessing is an enormous fact. A blessed person must be able to act as a master with the heart of "If I decide, the universe also decides" on behalf of God. Only with such conditions can heaven establish a living ideology centered on us.  
You must know how to protect the holy land and holy objects. You must devote all your efforts to protecting these. It seems you do not value blessed families. You must protect blessed families. You must find a holy land where you can live a holy life and die. You must quickly restore the holy land and holy people.  

4)  
Become a True Victor  
<Summary of Words> The one who wins and is elected in the presidential election must become a second victor who can contribute to humanity on the world stage.  
Jacob had to win over Esau in the second course after winning the first course in Haran.  
For Moses, rescuing the Israelite nation from Pharaoh in the palace was the first course. However, one must not be satisfied with the first course. After crossing the Red Sea, one must also win in the second course.  
Today, the first course has ended in victory. However, one must not be satisfied with this. Now we must go on to the second course of victory.  
It has been seven years since the teacher was released from prison. Let us go beyond these seven years and take a new path. It is regrettable that people seven years ago could not stand in this position. Therefore, you must do this work. Older people are caught up in their livelihoods.  
Many people who were willing to die have come and gone during the teacher's 42-year life. God wishes to give a worldwide blessing, but if families collapse, their descendants cannot have a greater path. There are not such great expectations for blessed families either.  

5)  
Become a Soldier for National Restoration  
Unification Church members should not be deceived by the words that attending their church will lead to prosperity. Those who say such things all have the mindset of thieves.  
It takes at least five years for a household that has collapsed to recover to some extent, but can a country, especially one as chaotic as Korea, be restored in just a few months? Absolutely not.  
Restoring the nation and its timeline  
Even if a household collapses, it requires more than five years to correct it; how much more time is needed to restore a nation that has fallen? It requires more than ten years, right? Moreover, we have the tremendous ideal of saving the nation, the world, and the universe. If so, do you think we can revive the management of this universe and return this world to its original state in three years? If you think it can be done in three years, you have the mindset of a true thief. It absolutely cannot be done.  
Then can it be done in seven years? It cannot be done in seven years either. Even the Almighty God has spent 6,000 years making countless sacrifices to correct this, and yet it has not been corrected; can weak humans correct it in seven years and establish the original ideal standard? It cannot be done.  
Then, looking at this Republic of Korea, to make it a nation that does not fall behind any advanced country in the world and can lead in all aspects, it will take at least 40 years, even if our thirty million people unite. Think about it. How long does it take to build a large building? Therefore, it will take 40 years.  
Today, while riding in the car, I talked about the pyramids of Egypt. You know the pyramids? They are about 150 meters high, and they contain about two million large stones that cannot be moved even by dozens of people. It took about 100,000 people working for 40 years to build one pyramid. Now, how long will it take to establish the Republic of Korea in a complete position, a sovereign nation that can shine brightly in history and remain forever? Do you think it can be done in 40 years? It requires more than 40 years of hard work to achieve that.  
Then, what kind of person can lead this nation? It must be a person who can raise a stick and say to thirty million people, "You all suffer. You cannot eat, you cannot live, and even in the face of death, endure." Only such a leader can save this nation. The teacher knows this fact. Do you understand what I mean? Those with thought will understand.  
Therefore, the teacher's purpose in leading the Unification Church is different from the purposes of the people of the world. We have already begun our march toward that destination. And since the teacher stands in the position of leading that march, there are many twists and turns along the way. When the wind and rain lash, the person at the forefront bears the brunt of it. All twists and obstacles must be resolved through him. This is the principle. Therefore, it is undoubtedly a fact that the position of the teacher leading the Unification Church is more difficult than that of those following.  
So what is our purpose today? The signboard of the Unification Church is not the problem. There may come a day when we can take that signboard down overnight. Our goal is to establish a sovereign nation that can shine light on the three thousand li peninsula and the world and make this nation a good people, a historical nation, and make the three thousand li territory a historical territory.
What should the Unification Church members do? They must take the lead and assume responsibility. To do this, what must they do? As mentioned earlier, those who take the lead are the ones who play the role of leaders, and leaders must face all obstacles first. Therefore, you must endure all the difficulties and storms of this nation first. Only then can you fulfill a leadership mission before that nation. This is the principle.

The purpose of our struggles
The purpose of making you suffer is not the teacher's intention. What will be accomplished by making you walk this path of hardship? While others live comfortably and lazily, what is the reason for pushing you out of your comfortable nests to seek a path that is tragic, lonely, sad, and stormy? It is to walk the path of pioneers and leaders so that the entire nation can emulate that courage and spirit. Someone must do it. At first, it will be one person, then two, then three, and in this way, the entire thirty million must move in that direction. Such determination must be instilled from parents to their young children. A mother must be able to forget her own difficulties while holding her baby and nursing it, praying for a moment of victory for this nation. We have taken on this tremendous mission.

We have come this far after three years, but this is not the end. The teacher who leads you is also not ending after three years. He thinks he must continue to lead and run even more. In the past, we rode bicycles, but now we are determined to stand at the forefront and run using the greatest achievements of civilization. No matter what enemy blocks our path, we are resolved to overcome it.

To return the world to God and to turn the evil world into a good world, we must inevitably go through a history of struggle.

When people are asked what their wishes are, most will respond that they wish they had more money because they were born into a poor family. They might say they wish they had power because they were born into a powerless family. They might say they wish they could study because they were born into a poor family and could not study like others.

I have met you for the first time in several months, and among you, there may be some who wonder if the teacher will bring some food or a burden for you. There may be those who think it would be better to receive bread than words because they are hungry. I apologize to those people, but the teacher did not bring a bundle of bread. He did not come to give you bread. He did not come to make you drowsy.

Then what did he come to give? Just as the teacher has a purpose for coming here, you also have a purpose for being here. What must these two purposes combine to accomplish? There is a mission and responsibility that must be fulfilled. Is that right? Both the teacher and you came here with a purpose. Do you understand?

Now, hundreds of people have gathered around me, and you and I are engaged in a kind of struggle. When I stand here, the teacher disregards you. Even in such a situation, you must create an environment where you can say you are right. Otherwise, you cannot be uplifted. Do you understand what I mean?

To make you better, you must be supplemented, but how should you be supplemented? You must uproot everything and cut off the branches before you can provide something new. Therefore, you must disregard your personality. The teacher must help you become better. That is the responsibility of the teacher.

You may think, "Is this the first time seeing the teacher, and he only speaks such harsh words right away?" There are many things he could say, but he only speaks words that disregard our personalities. However, think carefully. Was what he said earlier a lie? It is indeed the case. Therefore, I hope you will stay focused for one hour. I must either pack my bundle and leave or you must bow your heads.

What people have pursued and what is currently needed
Now, let’s go back to what we were discussing earlier. I asked that young woman what she wanted to become, right? Nowadays, when you ask young people what they want to do, some respond that they want to become the richest person in Korea. Then, some say they wish they could control Korea, meaning they want to become the president and hold the power of the nation in their hands to lead thirty million people. Next, they might say they want to become an unparalleled scholar whom the whole world admires and cannot follow. Most people aim for these three things. Human desires are money, power, and knowledge. Summarizing, that is the case. Is that right?

Then, when asked what is most necessary and urgent for saving this country and this nation, people say it is money. They say there must be an economic foundation. Next, they say it is power. Thus, they say, "Ah! We must seize sovereignty." Then they say we must raise the cultural level. They say we must elevate the people’s morality. All of this makes sense.

However, can money save a nation forever? No. Can power save a nation forever? No. Can knowledge save a nation forever? Neither can that. No matter how high the knowledge is, unless it can bind the hearts of many people and become the cornerstone of national spirit, that knowledge may help at some point, but it cannot become the eternal foundation for creating a cultural world. What all humanity desires are money, power, and knowledge. Those are what the 20th-century civilization was built upon.

Now let’s think about America today. America has an economic foundation that all nations envy, and it is based on democracy that all nations admire. It stands as a civilized nation, a developed country that others cannot follow. However, is America truly in a position to save the democratic camp? No, it is not. Is it in a position to save the world? No, it is not. The same goes for communism. So now, while democracy and communism shape the trends of the world, can these two ideologies once again organize human history and restore the scattered conscience of humanity to establish an unchanging foundation in heaven and earth? They cannot. It is impossible. Now, the Soviet Union is discarding the prestige of the international communist party and is degrading into a nationalist communist party.

Then, what should the young men and women who think correctly desire at this time? It is neither money nor power nor knowledge. No matter how much you fight for those things, they are transient. You cannot rely on such things. What is needed? We need people who can make those with money feel ashamed, people who do not bow down to those in power, and who can think, "Though you command me now, in ten years or several decades, I will surely make you submit."

We need people who may not have knowledge or power but possess the greatest and most historical truth, people who can say they have the ultimate truth that cannot be exchanged for heaven and earth. If such a group emerges, they will surely cause a worldwide event.

Such people cannot be pushed away by any power in the world. No one can move them from their position. No one has the authority to do so. If there is someone who can confidently say they possess the fundamental truth that can grasp the source of the conscience world that others do not know, encompassing and binding conscientious living and circumstances, then surely all of humanity throughout history will worship them. Even the saints and sages who have come to this earth will have to bow before them, and the people of this era will automatically establish the noun "submission" before them and will have no choice but to follow silently. That is how it will be.

Wealth, power, and knowledge are all transient
So, what path should we Unification Church members take? What path should the teacher who guides you take? What path must one take to live a truly human life? One must not become a person who sells their personality for material gain, nor should one sell their knowledge for material gain, nor should one sell their personality or the truth they respect for power. One must not be able to sell or move their personality or children, but rather should be able to say that the only thing they can move is the great way of heaven and earth, and they will only move according to that great way. If there is such a person, they can turn the wheels of history that are entering the realm of death in a new direction, can organize all the systems of a chaotic society, and can lead the traditions of society in one direction.

Then, what did our Unification ideology standardize and start from? It did not start from the worldly desires that humans seek. It started by stepping on that. The teacher does not envy those who possess worldly things. He does not envy those who sit in the position of millionaires and boast of what they have, nor does he envy those who command with power. He does not envy those who boast of having any ideology or knowledge that creates a new culture. You must also disregard such things and rise above them to contemplate the fate of history that must be settled. Such things will surely pass. You cannot place any attachment, desire, or emotion on them. This is an inevitable fact. Therefore, we must disregard such things and start from above them.

Then, what knowledge do we need? It is not visible worldly knowledge. It is not knowledge needed to prepare a place of comfort centered on the flesh. Nor is the authority we pursue worldly authority. It is the authority that can be revered by all creation based on that conscience and personality. And what kind of material do we desire? It is pure and undefiled material that exists as it was created by God, based on justice. Unless people or organizations, or any ideology or thought that moves based on such things emerge, this world will perish. It will be destroyed and collapse.

What was the purpose for which the teacher has fought for 40 years, risking his life? The teacher did not want money. What did he want? He wanted true people. What kind of true people? People who can cut off temporary desires and rebuild with their right arms. That is the kind of people he wanted. For this reason, our Unification Church has walked a miserable path. However, the teacher who leads the Unification Church did not think it was miserable. Even in a position where all people look upon, mock, curse, and criticize, the teacher did not lose hope. He did not envy any worldly environment. All of that will pass anyway.

Even if Americans boast of their economic power to the world, that too does not belong to them. It does not belong to America. No matter how much America commands the world based on the sovereignty of democracy, that power is not America’s own power. Even if there is a cultural nation that can command and organize heaven and earth, the foundation of that culture and knowledge does not belong to that nation.

The economic power that can remain at the end of history, the authority that can remain at the end of history, the knowledge that can remain at the end of history—these are the things that will be buried in history. The economic power, authority, and knowledge that can last alongside history are those that have an owner. That owner is God. Therefore, none of these belong to humans; they all belong to God.

That is why people call upon God with their hearts. They are also demanding their own standards that resonate in heaven. Therefore, the conscience continuously rejects the direction in which the body is heading unless it is good, and it has been accusing until now. This is because that is the path that those who yearn for heaven and live centered on heaven must take.

For this reason, the more money you have, the more you should want to give to others. The more power you have, the more you should want to turn it into the property of all people. If you have discovered the source of true knowledge that cannot be repaid even if you give the world, you should want to turn it into the property of the world. This is the desire that a person should originally have. However, since the world is not like that, it all collapses. This is an ironclad rule.

Justice remains, and injustice falls
Today, when the teacher of the Unification Church stands before you, the words he speaks are not his own. I know that there is a heavenly principle that has remained with history and will organize reality and lead history. Therefore, I constantly think about how to guide the Unification members onto the path of the heavenly principle that can remain, how to establish them as beings that can remain, and how to allow them to settle on an eternal foundation of rest that the conscience desires and the world of heart longs for, leaving behind the highest truth for which even millions can be grateful.

In this light, where should we drive the members of the Unification Church? We must drive them along this path. Knowing this, the teacher has walked that path and fought until now. As long as the blood in my body does not dry up and my nerves do not sever, what I see and feel is different.

I do not know God and am not seeking Him as the world does today. I do not desire the environment they boast of as a place of comfort. I do not desire a position of commanding with power. I am starting from a different direction and a different standard. Therefore, there is a conflict. But let’s try it. Justice remains, and injustice falls. The leaves of a branch with life remain. However, the leaves of a branch that has lost its life fall.

The fate of heaven and earth eternally revolves. Now is the time to push towards a new history. However, if one can only equip themselves with a personality that can align with that direction, even if history passes and all the cultures, powers, and economic strengths of the world disappear, the standards they hope to establish will surely remain. This is principle and heavenly law.

What should we do with the members of the Unification Church? We must drive them toward that path. The economic perspective and standards of authority that heaven and earth desire are different from those of the world. The highest standards of knowledge and truth that heaven and earth seek to establish are also different from worldly standards. We must also move forward from that standpoint. If we do so, there will be nothing to envy. That is why I am leading you forward.

Then, in what position can we meet true people? In this society that is collapsing, in this trend that is failing, amidst this chaos, those who are laughing and enjoying themselves...
Can we meet in the village? No.
Then what kind of person is a true person? A person who looks at this world and cries, who looks at this world and harbors resentment, who believes this era must perish, and if it does not, will make it perish by their own hands, is a person who holds a heart based on justice. Such a person is a true person.
To meet such a person, what position must one stand in? One must stand in the most miserable position on this earth. Those who have money, those who have power, those who have knowledge have tried to establish their position with what they have. But do those people truly understand the value of money? Do they truly understand the value of power? Do they truly understand the value of knowledge? They do not. However, when they stand in the opposite position, they can protect that value one hundred percent and can uphold it one hundred percent.
Does goodness come from the world? No. Does it come towards me? No. Goodness comes from behind. Therefore, it is said to act with goodness. If one cannot grasp the direction to turn while holding onto the center of the heavenly fortune when the wheel of history turns, when it turns past 180 degrees, it will fall away and self-destruct because it has no relation to that axis (center).
In developed countries, there is much money, but whose money is it? It is God's. Whose power is it? It is God's. Whose knowledge is it? It is God's. Then who is God? He is the Father of all people. Therefore, the character, economy, power, and truth of that Father belong to all people. This is why democracy has emerged in recent times.
In democracy, sovereignty belongs to the people, that is, to all people. Therefore, it is said that the people must control sovereignty. However, today it is said that sovereignty belongs to the people, but in reality, that sovereignty is held by the conglomerates. Right now, America is well-fed, but it cannot prosper alone. Everything must be shared. Because of this, America must provide aid to foreign countries. Otherwise, it cannot survive. Everything that America has is not just for America; it belongs to the world. No knowledge is exclusive to developed countries. It belongs to the world.
Even when giving, it must be done with the heart of a parent, shedding tears.
Now, what must America do? It must release its economic power and go to the poorest countries with the heart of a parent. Otherwise, it will perish. It must give sincerely, from the position of a servant, while shedding tears. When giving to those who are crying, one must stand in the position of those who shed tears. In giving, one must not give from the position of power that they have held until now. Otherwise, there will be backlash. Who should shed tears first? It should not be the receiver who sheds tears first, but the giver who must shed tears first. That is the position of a parent. Therefore, the giver must give while shedding tears. That is the way it should be.
When a parent sees their child in a miserable and cruel position, they only think of going to that child while shedding tears. If the great way of heaven and earth is like that, then moving in that direction is the principle. The one who has is the elder brother and the steward. Therefore, everything must be shared.
Then how should one give? It must be given with tears. If one gives while mocking, they will perish. This must be understood. America occasionally provides aid, but if it does so with power, it will perish. That is the principle. The same goes for the Republic of Korea. When America boasts of having provided aid, it should not say, "When have you ever received?" Giving must be done with tears. If one cannot become a person who can give with tears, they are not siblings but enemies.
Money is the enemy. The teacher has realized this many times, which is why he can shed tears wanting to give and is trying to create people who can truly give while shedding tears. Heaven is looking for such people. Cultivating such character is more necessary than worldly money or worldly power. Heaven turns the fortunes of heaven and earth in such a position. Therefore, if a nation does not become such a nation, it will soon be absorbed by another nation. Considering this, we should give even if we are unhappy. Even when giving, we should give with tears. If that is not enough, we should give with blood. We should give with tears, sweat, and blood.
If God exists, whom among the people of the world would He seek out and whom would He justify? If I were God, I would seek out such a person. However, looking at this world now, there are those who have, those who wield power, and those who claim to know something, but there is no one who truly wants to share with tears, who wants to embrace with tears, who wants to help with tears, who wants to teach with tears. Therefore, this world must perish.
Then where does the Unification Church want to go? Where does it want to go? The sorrow of heaven, the sorrow of history, and the sorrow of the times are not because there is no money, nor because there are no people, nor because there is no power. It is not because culture has not developed, or because there is a lack of knowledge. It is because those who have money do not truly know how to share, those who have power do not truly know how to protect, and those who know do not truly know how to teach. Therefore, we must understand that the world is corrupt and perishing.
Then what should we do to prevent such a world? We must go beyond the ideology of democracy and adopt the ideology of globalism. If there are nations that America cannot give to, we must have the heart to give first. Even if giving just a piece of bread, we must give it with our utmost effort and spirit, from a place where our bones are melting. When that piece of bread is given, the nation will receive it and wail. When they realize that we have come a long way for the sake of a poor nation, transcending regions and distances with heartfelt steps, even if they lose the piece of bread they brought, even if they collapse and wail from exhaustion along the way, history will elevate them, and that place will become the foundation of traditional national character and new ideology for future generations. This is the law of heaven and earth that you must understand.
The giver is greater than the receiver.
Until now, I have said, "Father, do not give me money." If I were to earn money, I could earn enough not to owe anyone. Money is necessary, but more necessary is the person who conquers money. We need someone who can come and say, "Please use this as well." Therefore, Unification members must become givers. The giver is more admirable than the receiver.
When I go on tour to the regions, I can see that the lives of our members are miserable. Wherever I go, I know there are members who cannot eat or wear what they need and are suffering. Men must suffer in place of Jesus, and women must suffer in place of the Holy Spirit. Just as the Holy Spirit worked hard on the earth, women must devote themselves to raising their families. Husbands and wives must report their efforts to God and plead for their will to be fulfilled quickly. Families must set an example and establish traditions.  
Mothers must pray earnestly. If they do not fulfill their responsibilities, substitutes will be appointed.  
Just as you must not let the Teacher go hungry, you must not let blessed families go hungry. Blessings are given on behalf of God, so you must feel heartbroken about their hunger. If you do this, the thirty million people will have no choice but to follow us.  
This nation must stand in a position that cannot be without the ideology of the Unification Church. We must make Korea a priestly nation that can command all nations. Even if we fall, we must hold onto the thirty million people and fall.  
The seven-year great tribulation is for the restoration of individuals, for the restoration of families, etc.
It is necessary to go seven times for seven years. However, if you trust the teacher and go, you can finish it in just seven years. After the Second World War, I intended to go after seven years, but due to a setback, I ended up coming out through prison.

The 21 years of hardship that Jacob endured in Haran can now be completed in a period of four years. This period only happens once. The teacher is praying for you to quickly pass through the period of suffering, just as he did. You must go for the nation, and the teacher for the world.

The day when everything is offered to God will determine God's day. There have been countless days in heaven and earth, but there has not been a day for God. When we defeat Satan and overcome all difficulties, giving glory to God, God's creation ideology will be completed, and all children will greet the glorious day. We must hasten the arrival of this day.

Let us swear to this. Let us consider it an honor to be mobilized for this purpose. Such a person is the victor among victors and the most filial among the filial. Therefore, let us become people whom God can personally call filial.

**The Mission of World Unification and Family**

**<Summary of the Message>** Even when looking at individuals, the body and mind are not unified. This struggle must come to a conclusion. Because people are fighting, heaven and earth are also in conflict.

Centered on goodness, happiness and unhappiness are intertwined. Even if a person's heart and body are unified, the family, nation, heaven and earth, and God and humanity must also be unified.

People desire to be good and happy, but they must also strive to make those they meet good and happy. If an individual sacrifices for the happiness of the family, that is good. If the family sacrifices for the happiness of the nation, that is also good.

Then, whose true goodness is it? It can be said that goodness belongs to someone above oneself, namely God. Just because I give to someone above me does not mean that goodness disappears. It is because when the higher person is pleased, I can also be pleased. Happiness cannot be found in the individual, so it must be sought in a higher place.

The point of evil lies in the external. However, as long as God exists, the evil will perish, and only the good will remain. Therefore, democracy and communism cannot coexist. The better will remain. Thus, when a world of ideals higher than democracy comes, democracy will disappear.

When viewed from the center of God, the foundation of goodness is love. When there is love, unity is achieved automatically. If one loves at a level higher than Satan, even Satan will be drawn in. God created heaven and earth to give the highest goodness and love. Only by giving can one truly feel love.

God is the lord of all things. Therefore, humans become lords when they become one with God. Humans were created to give and receive well, but they have fallen into a position where they cannot give or receive. Herein lies the beginning of unhappiness.

The reason a person seeks to meet good people is to meet God through better people, and seeking good things ultimately aims to meet God. Finding the way to approach God is joy.

If one can receive one and give ten, it is as if one has multiplied ten children. Unity is achieved when there is a subject that can give when it wants to give and an object that can receive when it wants to receive.

God has no object to give to. God has been searching for an object to give to until now. However, the more humans are given, the more they become angry. Therefore, God has placed the closest noun to humans as an object to give, which is the noun of children.

The Lord comes to receive all of God's love and share it with humanity. Therefore, He comes as the True Parents in human form. Since it is said that unity is achieved through love, He must become either my bride or my parent. Thus, He appears as the embodiment of the highest happiness and the highest love. When a relationship is established with Him, one can gain strength many times over oneself.

Jesus called God the Parent and Himself the bridegroom and brother of humanity. This speaks to the importance of family. Heaven is a unified world centered on families that are centered on God. The world that expands the family is the earthly paradise. In that world, just hearing the words naturally draws the heart.

The demands of the heart for the body are infinite. Likewise, the heart gives infinite commands to the body because the infinite God is the subject. The heart must fully possess God's love to end its demands.

We must learn how to become filial sons and daughters, loyal subjects and virtuous women. Only then can we become filial sons and daughters to the Lord who comes, and loyal subjects and virtuous women to God. The Unification Church is the place that teaches this.

If the thief on the right had not died with Jesus, salvation might not have been achieved. God desires for humans to return to their homeland.

Having lost the original rights of family, tribe, nation, and world, we must again seek and achieve this creation purpose. The one who comes with this purpose is the Lord of the Second Advent. The first hope of fallen humans is to return to God's side; the second hope is to reclaim heaven and earth as their own; the third hope is to repay their enemies.

The original responsibility lies with God, who is the Parent. He sought to graft us from the position of God's servants to Jesus. Therefore, the words that Jesus brought to graft us are called the gospel.

Externally, the Israelite nation was unfaithful, and internally, Judaism was unfaithful, which caused them to lose their homeland. The Israelite nation was to become the people of Jesus and establish the territory and sovereignty of that nation.

To create a tribe centered on the King of Kings, Judaism was to become filial sons and daughters, and the Israelite nation was to become loyal subjects and virtuous women. The nation of Judah was a vassal state of Rome, so if they had established Rome in their hearts, they could have unified the world in one purpose. However, that did not happen, and the nation became wanderers. They lost their homeland in the First Eden and missed their opportunity in the Second Israel, thus living in the historical spiritual Canaan.

History is forming an era of simultaneity, leading to a Second Israel centered on spiritual ideals. Today's Christianity is in the position of Judaism from 2,000 years ago. Democracy must establish a world centered on Christianity.

Korea is in a position similar to that of the nation of Judah, while the United States is in a position similar to that of Rome. Korean Christianity represents the internal Judaism that symbolizes the internal Israel, and Korea is in the position of the internal Israel nation. Just as Israel was a vassal state of Rome, Korea is under the economic and cultural dominance of the United States.

However, due to their disbelief, the Unification Church has had to walk the path of Golgotha like Jesus. Nevertheless, we have triumphed here.

What was intended to be done in seven years has been extended to 21 years. Jacob had to work 14 years to take a wife and another 7 years to find all things. We must, like Jacob, seek children and material possessions to find the global Canaan.

Our church has been registered as having won against Christianity that opposes us. It has also been registered in the United States, so now we can find our original home centered on the expectation of the son-in-law.

The joint wedding ceremony is being held to resolve the historical resentment, and through this, we can find our original family. The fate of heaven and earth has begun to revolve around this.

Since Jesus could not hold the Israelite nation in His palm, we must walk the path of four years to make up for this.

Now there will be a great migration. Just like in the times of Jacob, Moses, and Jesus, this world will certainly return to God, and the day of offering will be God's day. By giving rewards to sons and daughters, a way for people of the world to enter has been prepared.

Just by participating in this period, you will be able to surpass other nations of the world. It is now 5:45 PM. Let us make our final resolution. To do so, we must endure hardship.

Among our ancestors, there were no true filial sons and loyal subjects.

102   The Path of Worship

What kind of being am I?
<Summary of the Message> Until now, you have made vows to face death with the will in front of you and have struggled through difficult circumstances along with those vows. You may not know it, but the results have greatly contributed to solidifying our foundation before this nation, and the teacher knows this well. While I am grateful for those who have worked hard, I want you to understand that my heart is to encourage those who feel the mission to understand the will but cannot go.

I am a historical being standing at the crossroads of good and evil.
Regardless of the era, even if people are asleep, history is moving in the direction of restoration providence. This is a fact that can be seen by looking at past history. 
Those living in that era may not have known due to ignorance or being in an evil generation, but the historical direction of that era has always moved toward a certain destination. 
Because there is God who manages the era and leads it, history is moving toward one destination. This fact can be inferred from our historical development.

Today, you know that I, as a being, is extremely precious and important. I also know well that I must be both a product of history and a current existence, as well as a source for the future. 
I am now at a crossroads of whether I will become the true me today or not. When I cry out for truth and try to hold onto true values, there are universal issues involved, and when I stand in an evil position, there are historical evils involved. You must always keep in mind that you are in such an environment.

Thus, the nation as a being stands at a crossroads where it can be good on the right side and evil on the left side, and this is, of course, the position of ordinary people who cannot escape the historical environment, and you must clearly realize that your position, knowing the will, is also the same. 
It is natural logic that after knowing the will, one must establish a good self centered on that will. However, we who know the will sometimes fail to become a good self and may unknowingly stand in the opposite position. When certain relationships and social environments surround us, we often experience going in the opposite position, either unknowingly or knowingly.

Planning process, preparation process, implementation process.
Then how should you proceed centered on yourself, standing at such a crossroads? 
Everyone has a period of thought. After thinking, if you decide that it is right, you need a period to prepare yourself based on your own determination or vow. It is through this preparation period that victory or defeat is ultimately determined. You go through the practical process of succeeding or failing during this preparation period.

Everyone, without exception, has a conscience. Conscience moves based on good, so a person who thinks centered on conscience will always think of the true. Preparing and practicing the true is the original duty of humanity. 
If that is the case for humans, then the Creator who created heaven and earth must also be so. There must have been a period of thought before creating heaven and earth, and there must have been a period of preparation as well. 
Before God made a decisive plan to create all things, there was first a period of thought. After that, based on that established plan, He went through a preparation process and moved on to the implementation stage. This is how He created heaven and earth.

That heaven and earth creation means that God is such a being. It means that God also had a period of thought, a period of preparation, and a period of implementation. He created all things through such a process. 
Then, who can be the central responsible person established in the implementation stage? It is humanity. There was a creation period of five days as a preparation period to create this humanity, and after laying the foundation of victory in the world of the heart centered on that period, He went through a preparation process and came to the implementation stage. God had to fight in the inner world of the heart and had to fight in preparation as well. Just as we humans do, God has walked out from such a position until now.

The practical mission is something that God must fulfill internally and humans must fulfill externally. When God, the subject of internal victory, presents internal conditions and commands before humans, the subject of external victory, humans must act, and there will inevitably be struggles involved. This struggle is the responsibility of humanity. However, because our human ancestors failed in the practical process, the result of the fall has led countless humanity today to face a fate where they must think again, prepare again, and practice again.

Therefore, today, anyone with a conscience cannot help but think, and after thinking, cannot help but prepare, and after preparing, cannot help but go through the process of struggle centered on external environments. Otherwise, victory or defeat will not be determined. This process is the position of humanity today, standing at the crossroads of pioneering the path of fate that has been reproduced.

The path that a person pursuing truth must take.
Now, what should you think? Of course, you should think of what I like and what I can be satisfied with. However, while it is our mission to think, prepare, and practice with the joy of the individual in mind, thinking of good things, preparing good things, and practicing good things does not start and end with oneself. The better it is, the more we must recognize that it is connected from me to the universe. Goodness does not start from my personal standards and bear fruit. It goes through the world of relative relationships to bear fruit. If there is to be a true person in the future, that person has the responsibility to lay the foundation on behalf of all people. A true person bears historical responsibility, so they must have a heart that connects the past, present, and future and must stand in a position where they can connect the values of the past, present, and future.

Then why do our hearts want to stand in such a position and seek such things? It is because God, who moves the heavenly principles, is in such a position. Because our inevitable fate is connected to the necessity of becoming an external entity to fulfill the practical mission, our hearts cannot help but move in that direction. If you observe that your hearts are moving in this way, no one can deny that we were born for a greater good and that our purpose in life is to live as a value-laden existence representing history, the times, and the future.

God can only conduct the final judgment centered on at least one national sovereignty. Because this is the standard of providence, there can be no law of forgiveness when we are in the time of establishing that national sovereignty.

Now, let us think of Noah through history. In his time, Noah was considered a fool and a simpleton. However, he was someone who could think of the past, the present, and the future. The world in which Noah lived was an evil world, and he could not remain there as it was. So, he sought the right time, found the true person suitable for that time, and hoped that this true person would guide him. However, since there was no one to guide him, he received heaven's permission to bear that responsibility himself.

For this reason, Noah was a person who thought when others did not, prepared for what others did not, and practiced what others failed to do. Abraham was the same, as were Moses, Jesus, and the Teacher. They all thought of what others did not think of, prepared for what others did not prepare for, and practiced what others did not practice.

The Teacher has brought the Unification Church to the stage where decisive practices must be made on a national standard. But have you, after entering the Unification Church and living a life of faith, ever thought, prepared, and practiced for the purpose like Noah did, or like the Teacher did? Have you devoted your entire life, whether you are awake or asleep, eating or dressing, coming or going, happy or sad, to this cause? If not, heaven cannot work for you.

You must not say, "I was like this in the past, I am like this today, so I will be like this in the future." The past version of you cannot be recognized in this era. If you have become a national self that can prove the past and the present, and can manage the past and the present, there is no problem. However, if you are dominated by the past and also dominated by the present, heaven cannot work there.

We must take on the mission that should replace Adam. 

You are moving, but you are not developing. However, the Teacher is developing. God has seemed to retreat in the providence of restoration until now, but has actually progressed. It may seem like a descent, but it has been an ascent.

So what time is it now? Until now, we have faced trials coming from individuals, families, or the entire nation. Within the framework of the Unification Church, we have faced external trials. However, since we have become a remnant there, we have become a group that can represent the nation, the ethnicity, and the religion. Therefore, even if we encounter the global flow, we must remain as a remnant here; otherwise, the Unification Church cannot stand as a global Unification Church, nor can it command on behalf of all sovereigns.

Thus, what must you understand through this gathering? Until now, you have received heaven's cooperation within the framework of religion and have fought external trials and struggles on that religious foundation, but now you must fight as the embodiment of God in place of God.

Adam had a mission to represent God. However, Adam could not fulfill that mission. Now, we must take responsibility for that mission in this era. You must become individuals who are filled with that conviction; otherwise, you cannot push forward the national fortune of today. You must understand this.

Until now, God has pushed you forward. When you fought, heaven and earth cooperated there. However, now you must fight as one, without heaven's cooperation, as the center representing heaven on this earth and as you representing the earth.

We must remember the fact that God told Adam and Eve to govern all things. Today, there must be a resolute determination that wherever in the cosmos God’s word is, we will go. If you do not possess that driving force that no one can hinder, you will fall along the way. You will retreat along the way.

Now, we Unification Church members must cry out to follow my example. I am a person who represents God, and since I have decided to fight on behalf of God, you must follow my example. In the heart of such a person, there is only the determination to conquer the world of enemies, and their entire life becomes a period of preparation for that. Once prepared, they fight without hesitation. If you are captured by the conviction to do so, there is nothing you cannot accomplish.

However, the difficult part is that this connects to the spirit world. Do you know what those who are spiritually connected demand? They want to be involved in the movements of the Unification Church. That is their current demand.

Recently, some people have reported to the Teacher that many spirits have come and asked when they can join in, expressing their desire to participate. However, the Teacher hopes to do this through you rather than doing it himself. He wishes that the authority to join them is not only granted by him but also by everyone who works for this purpose.

The Teacher hopes that you will be able to command on behalf of the countless martyrs, loyal subjects, virtuous women, and prophets who have worked for this purpose.

Another definition of the line

So, what must you do to become someone who can grant such privileges? Your ideology, which thinks of this era and the future, must align with God's heart.

Therefore, if possible, the Teacher wants to put you forward and remain behind. If the blessed individuals stand fully representing their families before the purpose, centered on God's heart, then the cosmos will turn around.

It is not a matter of a specific locality. People suffer because they are like a bunch of rascals, being pushed around by the wind. Such people, no matter how hard they work and prepare, cannot connect with the spirit world.

For those who are determined to go out and win under the conviction of fighting in the practical process of struggle, hunger is not an issue. God will never let such a person go hungry. The Teacher has experienced this. If you try to live in this world without fighting and seek shortcuts, you will only suffer and collapse.

God is trying to entrust a significant responsibility to us today. In such a time, examine yourself critically. Since I first entered the Unification Church, what have I done? What have I confronted for the purpose? Until now, all things have started from me and aimed to bear results from me. Is it right to say, "I have done this in the past, so I will do this in the future"?

The good things I have done must be given to the thirty million people, to humanity, to all people. If all things recognize and rejoice in that, then I will also rejoice. If they do not recognize it, I may feel disheartened, but even so, I must go with the heart to give.

If you do not have such a heart, when you go to the spirit world and God says, "Until now, I have worked hard for you, now you must work hard for me," how will you be able to lift your face?

God has entrusted us with the authority to rejoice in what we see. 

Ah! I am sad that I cannot possess that. I cannot rejoice because I have not achieved this. God does not say that. 

When you quietly observe the Unification Church youth today, they are trying to start from me and end with me. That is why they are failing. The Teacher is trying to uproot that root fundamentally without Satan knowing.

The line does not start and end with me; it starts from me and extends to countless others, rejoicing in their joy more than my own, and only then can I look at that and rejoice. If goodness does not exist in this way, then God is the ultimate dictator, and such a God is unnecessary.

Everyone, think quietly about yourselves today. Ask yourself if you are truly loyal and filial before God. Are you looking for a way to turn back when something is slightly unfavorable for you? If there are such individuals, the Teacher will not let them be.

The reason Israel fell lies right there. The reason Noah's family failed in the substantial offering lies there as well. Most of the children, families, or disciples who should have centered around the leaders who have been responsible for the providence of restoration have been like that. Where did the disciples who followed Jesus go? The very disciples who followed Jesus betrayed him. 

Today, among you, if there are those who think, "Ah! When a good era comes, I will become a prominent figure centered around our Teacher," they are all people who try to use heaven as a shield for their own success, centered on the world. There may be people who want to use goodness like that, but goodness will never be used. You must not use goodness. Goodness will never be used. It may seem like it is being used for a time, but ultimately, the one who uses it will perish. 

Those who use it will perish after using it.

The true meaning of completion

So, do you, who follow the purpose, want to turn the results of a good heart back to yourself? Or do you want to turn it back to all people? The distinction between good and evil occurs there, and the motivation for victory and defeat arises there.

A person who says, "Even if I die, I die for the whole, so please pass this on to my descendants for generations to come," is a good person. Those who try to use goodness for their own generation will not even surpass their own generation and will find their path blocked.

You must understand the meaning of the term "Seonghwa Youth Association." The term "Seonghwa" does not mean to harmonize passively due to some stimulus. It means to harmonize actively.

You have started with this meaning, yet in the morning you are happy, and by evening you are crying and making a fuss. Then at night, you do whatever you want, and that should not be the case. Those who know God's will should cry in the morning and rejoice in the evening or at night. Nevertheless, you initially rejoice but later make various conditions. That is why Seonghwa graduates are suffering so much.

If you could save the nation by hanging all of you on the cross at once, if you could save the nation by sending all of you to the front lines and pushing you into the pit of death, then that is the responsibility of both the Teacher and you. Therefore, what we have now...

No. I have beloved parents and siblings, and at the same time, there are nations and humanity, and there is heaven and earth. How serious is this issue? People might think it is someone else's issue, but at any moment, it could happen to me or my sons and daughters. Such things could happen in my family as well. No one can guarantee that they will not fall into such a fate. I cannot think that I am unrelated to it. All the tragedies that have occurred in history are not someone else's; they are mine. They are all my mission and my responsibility. Just because it has not happened around you does not mean you are unrelated. It is not like that.

So do not give your heart any gaps, and always be in a state of readiness so that when I give an order, you must take action one hundred percent in response to that order. You must become people who can do this. Now, you must recover the conviction that you can become this and shake the three thousand ri peninsula. Do you understand? Do you have that confidence?

<Summary of the Message> If we look at Korea geographically, the east where the sun rises represents masculinity, and the west where the sun sets represents femininity.

She had to fulfill the mission of a mother and the mission of a bride.

In the eastern region of Korea, there were three historians: Lee Yong-do, Hwang Guk-joo, and Baek Nam-joo. Baek Nam-joo came barefoot to Kim Seong-do, bowing and serving from the position of a servant. It is said that in the restoration era, a man must first come to serve a woman.

After 1920, an external spiritual history of men and women opposing the worship of shrines arose according to the internal history. If they had united with the Teacher at that time, the Teacher would not have suffered.
