However, you did not regard us as lacking, and even last year, you embraced us with love and made it a year without great twists.

Today, we welcome the first hour of the new day in 1964. Let us not forget that our lives are due to your hard work, and that our pride is due to the price of your blood.

We gather all our sincerity, take a solemn posture, and here are the sons and daughters who listen to the voice that comes from your heart, truly serving you. We will walk the path of death and any path of difficulty for the fulfillment of your desires.

Let us be sons and daughters who appeal to you with tearful hearts. How long have you awaited such sons and daughters?

This dawn, please look down upon your young children gathered here, Father.

When we think that there is a nation connected to this group, and that humanity is connected through this nation, and that the entire universe is connected to thousands of saints and all things, we believe that your joy is greater than the joy that comes from ourselves, and that it is the joy of the entire universe. We cannot help but feel that the responsibility and mission entrusted to us is too heavy.

As descendants of sin who have not escaped the traces of death, when we think about how we have left so many twists in heaven, we find it hard to have the courage to make promises and resolutions as we welcome the new year. However, because there are still many peaks of restoration that we must swear and go through, we feel that we must make new vows from this dawn before we even see the new light of the morning.

In this new year, with a new heart and new feelings, we vow to fulfill the responsibilities of a pioneer and a leader representing this nation and humanity, and may this vow we make move heaven. May we become new selves who can confront the forces of darkness with heavenly authority and the authority of love, and may the light of this vow be established today so that all 365 days of 1964 may be like this day.

May this new resolution and new determination of this year become the foundation of your glory and make us the helm of a ship crossing the river of suffering in the world of death. Thus, we sincerely hope that we will not feel obstacles or sufferings in reaching the garden of hope that you desire.

Even this dawn, there are family members scattered across South Korea who call upon your name with a heart full of intention, so please embrace them. Moreover, now, as we face a significant period in heaven, there are lonely family members who are welcoming the new year with tearful hearts, so may a new light of brightness shine upon them from this day, and may you grant us a day to elevate and illuminate the foundation of your glory. We sincerely hope that you will look upon the hearts of all the sons and daughters who bow their heads here this dawn and that we may welcome a new day with you.

As a group of unity, forgive the past sins of this nation, forgive the sins of humanity centered on this nation, and forgive the sins of all the grieving souls in heaven and earth, as well as the sins of our ancestors who have come and gone from the past to the present.

Please protect and guard the day of joy until this nation and we can manifest it to the world as a light of life. We sincerely hope and ask that the remaining days of victory come to us quickly and that the harsh conditions of the remaining battlefield disappear along with the light of life.

We hope that your glory may fill the entire universe and be with the blessed families, this nation, and countless people. We pray in the name of the Holy True Parents. Amen.

<Words> As we look forward to the four-year journey, we have received the message to become victorious subjectors as the slogan for the four years that God has entrusted to us.

To pave the ground for victory, you must understand that before seeking the victory of the whole, you must first lay the foundation for the victory of the individual. This victory is a noun that has been sought in the past, is being sought in the present, and must be sought in the future. It is a noun that God has sought, that the earth has sought, and that our ancestors have sought, but since the day of the fall until today, humanity and God have been unable to possess the noun of victory in the world of ideals created by God and have come out with the nouns of sorrow and misery.

There can be no complete victory until we completely eliminate all the conditions we do not want in our living environment.

God, who is carrying out the restoration providence, has also been fighting for victory until now. Likewise, our ancestors, who have borne the responsibility of heaven's will through the ages, have also fought for victory.

Through the long history of 6,000 years, we have awaited the day of victory, but even God has not yet welcomed that day. When we consider that we are still in a stage where we cannot say that we have the day of complete victory in this era that looks at the past, present, and future, we realize that we are still in a position where we must look forward to victory.

Each of us in this position must prepare for the greater victory we seek. We must once again think that we are in a position where we must make decisions, take action, and resolve to fight against our enemies.

God has encouraged our ancestors to believe in Him. After believing, they were to receive God's blessings and, on the foundation of the hope granted, become one with the love of the Father, thus becoming the eternal joy of the Father and the joy of humanity, and eternally the victory of the Father and the victory of humanity.

God has allowed humanity to reach such a position, but we have lost the faith granted by God, lost the hope granted by God, and lost the love granted by God. Therefore, this remains as God's wish in managing the restoration providence, and it also remains as humanity's wish to uphold the will of that providence. Thus, God's wish...
and humanity's wishes still remain in our individual selves today.  
In 1 Corinthians 13:13, it is stated that faith, hope, and love will always exist, but the greatest of these is love. However, God also hopes for faith, hope, and love. What is the most precious thing for humanity? It is advancing to the place of faith where God can believe, advancing to the place of hope where God can hope, and advancing to the place of love where God can love. This is the maximum happiness that humanity can enjoy. To establish this foundation of happiness, humanity has sought the faith that God can allow and the love that God can allow. This is something that must be found, but finding it is not an easy task.  
To establish personal faith, personal struggle is necessary. Based on the fulfillment of faith and hope, one must achieve God's love. To do this, one must set their own standard and establish an eternal relationship with God. You must understand that love cannot be found without struggle.  
**The Purpose of Faith, Hope, and Love**  
So, what is the purpose of faith, what is the purpose of hope, and what is the purpose of love? Of course, among these, all of creation is included, but more importantly, it is humanity, the central and core being of the universe created as God's representative who can govern heaven and earth. Humanity itself is the embodiment of the purpose of faith, the embodiment of the purpose of hope, and the embodiment of the purpose of love.  
1 Corinthians 13 is referred to as the chapter of love, and what is the ultimate purpose it signifies? It is humanity itself. Of course, before this world becomes the purpose, the nation must become the purpose, and before the nation becomes the purpose, the race must become the purpose, and before the race becomes the purpose, the individual, that is, oneself, must become the purpose.  
Then, what kind of human is the one around whom hope, faith, and love are centered? It is the person of hope that God envisioned at the time of creation, the perfect person who can move heaven and earth, and the true person in whom God can dwell.  
The words of such a person are words that move heaven and earth, the whispers of that person are whispers that resonate with heaven and earth, and the joys that person enjoys are joys shared with heaven and earth. It is for such a person that the term faith has emerged in our time.  
Today, fallen humanity is wandering in search of the ideals of hope and a focal point. But what is their ultimate purpose? It is to find a person who can rejoice with heaven and earth, communicate with heaven and earth, and reveal the glory of heaven. We must understand that such a person is the embodiment of the purpose of faith, the embodiment of the purpose of hope, and the embodiment of the purpose of love.  
You may know from learning the Principle of Restoration that all conditions for indemnity to establish faith or to shed fallen nature arise based on faith. To shed fallen nature, the Messiah, who is the embodiment of hope, must come. What have we been hoping for until now? It culminates not in fallen humanity but in the coming Messiah.  
The Messiah is the embodiment of the purpose of faith, the embodiment of the purpose of hope, and the embodiment of the purpose of love. When the purpose has been fulfilled centered on the Messiah, what will remain? Since all purposes have been achieved, only love can remain. Therefore, it is said that in the end, love remains. That love is the love through the completed embodiment of faith and the love through the completed embodiment of hope. We know that the one who comes as the representative of that love is the Messiah.  
So, in order for you to become victors, from what position must you become victors? You must become victors from the position centered on faith, and you must become victors from the position centered on hope.  
Humanity is hoping for a time when impossibility can become possibility. Because of that impossibility, they are searching for one person. In order to find that one person who is the embodiment of faith, hope, and love, fallen humanity is struggling. Therefore, when we cry out for faith, we need the embodiment of faith; when we cry out for hope, we need the embodiment of hope; and when we cry out for love, we need the embodiment of love.  
Who is the embodiment of faith, hope, and love? He is the true person who is not related to the world of fallen nature. Through him, heaven and earth are restored; through him, the glory of heaven begins; and through him, the love between the Father and the Son begins. Furthermore, through him, the connection of husband and wife centered on the relationship of parents and children, and the connection of family centered on that relationship, will lead to the new origin of heaven and earth. We must understand this.  
**The Messiah Who Comes as the Embodiment of Faith, Hope, and Love**  
That origin must begin through one embodiment, that is, the embodiment of the purpose of faith, the embodiment of the purpose of hope, and the embodiment of the purpose of love. When the time comes to welcome that person as the bridegroom, only the embodiment of love will be an issue, and a world centered on love will unfold. Therefore, we must understand that the Bible also speaks of this.  
Then how is the embodiment you desire, that is, the embodiment of faith, the embodiment of hope, and the embodiment of love, realized? It is not achieved all at once. To establish the embodiment of faith, one must connect with the fallen individual and establish a family through the hand of heavenly providence, building up tribes and nations to bring us to the present day. Many people in the past believed and followed, but they have not yet achieved the purpose of faith, they have not achieved the purpose of hope, and they have not achieved the purpose of love.  
So how can this be achieved? When the highest victor who can win through faith appears, when the highest victor who can win through hope appears, and when the highest victor who can win through love appears, then it will finally be achieved. You must understand this.  
Then who is the coming Messiah? He is the one who becomes the embodiment of faith, the embodiment of hope, and the embodiment of love. To become the embodiment of the purpose of faith, he must possess the qualifications of one who has won through historical struggles centered on faith. It cannot be done without merit. To become the embodiment of hope, he must have the value of one who has won in the historical struggle for global hope. The same applies to becoming the embodiment of love.  
When we look at each of us who are living a life of faith today, our individual purpose in seeking faith and hope may be to save the individual, to save the family, or even to seek the embodiment of faith for the tribe, nation, world, and heaven and earth. It is harder to save the family than the individual, harder to save the tribe than the family, and harder to save the nation than the tribe. The broader the scope, the harder it becomes to save.  
Who is the coming Messiah? He is the one who can stand as the embodiment of faith, hope, and love for not only individuals but also families, tribes, nations, the world, and the entire universe. Only when he stands in such a position can the faith that has remained in human history bear fruit, the hope bear fruit, and the love bear fruit. Otherwise, faith, hope, and love cannot bear fruit. The words he speaks are not personal words. You must understand that when you shout with such conviction, those words, though coming from an individual, will be words that have historical significance and connection.  
**The Attitude of the Saints Facing the End Times**  
Then how should you face this time of the end? God is determined to establish the final point of world history centered on the Messiah who comes as the embodiment of hope, faith, and love. Now, how should you prepare to meet such a time? Since he appears with global significance, you must also stand in the same position as him. The era centered on the individual, the era centered on the family has passed. Today is the era of globalism centered on a new owner. Life will also take place on the stage of globalism. In order to make you stand as the embodiment of faith, hope, and love on a historical scale, you must recognize the efforts of history.  
So what should you do? From your personal life to family, tribe, nation, and heaven and earth, you must be able to negotiate with God, saying, "Is this not the embodiment you desired?" If your actions cannot stand out on the historical stage as a significant part of the embodiment of faith, then you must become someone who can follow within that scope. You must have such inner resolve.  
Then how should you become? You must become one with the coming embodiment of faith, hope, and love. To do that, you must find your own faith that can weigh itself in relation to the one who is the embodiment of faith and hope.  
To do this, you must reflect on history. You must uncover historical connections and recognize that the end times of world history have come. You must also understand the values of the nation, the people, the race, the family, and the individual, and recognize that until now, individuals have been working to build the world.
We must seek the tradition of faith that has emerged through tribes, nations, and states. In faith, whether it is Abraham, Moses, or Noah, we must surpass their faith.

Noah believed for 120 years to save his family. He abandoned all the environments he was living in. Even his family members opposed him, but Noah transcended all of that. No matter how severe the persecution or how difficult the circumstances, Noah did not succumb. The same was true for Abraham. Leaving Ur of the Chaldeans, whether moving to Canaan or Egypt, he held the conviction that nothing in the world could be a problem in fulfilling his purpose.

The Mission of the Bride
To establish something that is better than our ancestors, we must understand that we have come out with hope in faith, fighting to be loved before heaven. When we think of this, you who are in the end times must not be inferior to them in terms of your daily lives or your determination. You must understand that being inferior to them means you cannot stand before the Lord who is coming as a bride.

So, what must we do to stand as a bride before the Lord who is coming? We must create an environment to welcome the bridegroom who will restore the world. We need to establish the expectations of faith as a bride on the foundation of world historical faith, so that the Lord, who is the bridegroom, can appear and fulfill His purpose upon that expectation. This has been the original purpose of laying the foundation of faith for 6,000 years, but until today, humanity has not achieved it. Rather, it has been destroyed. We must realize that there is no sadder thing than this.

Now that you know this, what should you do? Even if you cannot engage in historical struggles externally, you must embrace all historical struggles internally and go through the history of struggle that may leave the cross before the coming Lord. Only then can you appear before the Lord who comes as the reality of faith, the reality of hope, and the reality of love. This is the principle.

If you lay such a foundation to welcome the coming Lord, He will not suffer. If you prepare everything to welcome the bridegroom as a bride, the Lord who is the bridegroom will not suffer when He comes to this earth. By laying such a foundation, you will be able to stand in a position to enter the land of Canaan after passing through the path of Egypt and the wilderness, so there will be no pain or trials before the coming Lord. However, because all of this has not been accomplished, the coming Lord will come and undertake all the struggles that the bride must do.

When the Lord comes, from that day on, the day of the Lord begins, and we must lay the foundation of Canaan in preparation for this day. Despite this mission being present for believers, when they fail to lay the foundation of Canaan, the coming Lord must walk the path of tribulation and prepare the way that the brides must go. Today, the Unification Church is working to rectify this once again.

So, are you standing on the foundation of the complete purpose of faith? Are you standing on the foundation of the complete purpose of hope? Are you standing on the foundation of the complete purpose of love? No, you are not. There is still a path to walk. That is why we have entered an era where we can walk together with you. This is the path that started focusing on 1960. The believers on this earth, who are in the position of the bride waiting to welcome the Lord, have the responsibility to lay the foundation for the day of the purpose of faith, hope, and love, but because they have not fulfilled their responsibilities, they must once again establish the conditions for victory, starting from the individual, through the family, tribe, and nation.

The Path of Sorrow, Pain, and Misery for Victory
Today, we are raising the slogan to become victorious subjects. What is this victorious subject? It is a victorious subject regarding the past, a victorious subject when looking at the present, and a victorious subject regarding the future. We must become such individuals.

When we look back at our past today, we may have set the standard of a victorious subject in some fields. However, before this era, the absolute desire of history still remains. You must understand that this eternal path is still being left behind. That is why we are striving to become this victorious subject.

After going through the era of individual victory, we must move on to the era of family victory, the era of tribal victory, the era of national victory, and the era of victory on a global scale. In order to become the victorious subjects we desire, we must re-establish what Jesus attempted to set up, focusing on the heavenly sovereignty and the sovereignty of the earth, namely the sovereignty of Israel, to establish a day of victorious glory in the world.

Because Jesus could not stand on the victorious foundation of the nation and the people, He could not fulfill the providence of restoration. Therefore, we must strive to lay the victorious foundation of the nation and the people over the next four years. After this path is completed, we must also move on to become global victorious subjects.

God has worked tirelessly from the time of Cain until today through this historical path. In Noah's time, He sought to establish Noah as a victor but could not achieve it. The same was true in Abraham's time and Moses' time. It was the same after Jesus came and left. When we think about how they all remained in such relationships, each of you today has the responsibility to rectify everything centered on this era. If the teacher says he will take responsibility for you, you must take responsibility for the past, and if the teacher says he will take responsibility for the future, you must take responsibility for the present.

You must become victorious subjects in this historical path. However, until now, there have been no individual victorious subjects, family victorious subjects, tribal victorious subjects, national victorious subjects, or global victorious subjects. What God desires is a nation centered on one sovereignty, so we must fight centered on the Republic of Korea.

Achieving this will involve sorrow, pain, and misery. This path is a path of struggle, a path of pain, and a path of misery. These become the conditions for the whole. There cannot be a victory that ignores this. You must understand that. Noah was the same, Abraham was the same, and Jesus was the same. The nations that followed them were also poor nations, suffering nations, and miserable nations. This has been the process of weaving historical struggles until now. Therefore, to become victorious subjects, we must overcome the peaks of sorrow, the peaks of pain, and the peaks of misery.

The Stage of Overcoming Through Patience
To overcome these, what must we surpass? We must overcome with patience. Without patience, we cannot overcome. Therefore, we need to endure and bear, that is, we need patience.

What is the saddest thing for us? There is nothing sadder than losing beloved parents and spouses. Also, losing a nation or losing the world is the saddest thing. Then, conversely, what is joy? It is finding the lost parents, finding the spouse, finding the children, finding the siblings, finding the tribe, finding the nation, and finding the world. What then is suffering? It is being hungry, being naked, suffering from illness, and not being free. All of these sufferings must be overcome with patience.

The path to victory inevitably involves such things. Therefore, in the history of humanity, there is sorrow, pain, and misery that bleed. We must overcome these peaks. Those who retreat from the peak of sorrow can never advance to the peak of joy. Those who retreat from suffering cannot seize the joy that lies beyond suffering. Those who retreat from misery cannot seize the happiness that lies beyond misery. Today, the place we aim for in faith, hope, and love is a place that can only be found by stepping over sorrow, pain, and misery. You must understand this. This misery, pain, and sorrow are historical on a global scale.

Dear ones, in the world, if you set a goal and want to achieve it, there will be accompanying sorrow, pain, and misery. How much more so when trying to fulfill God's will? If you want to become the victorious subjects of hope, faith, and love, what must you do? You must not become a dropout by experiencing sorrows, pains, and miseries that are equal to that. Since we have taken on the responsibility of the purpose we are seeking, we must overcome whatever comes with patience.

That is why Jesus faced the sorrows and miseries that came with a global historical sentiment, a global historical belief, a global historical faith, a global historical wish, and a global historical love. We too must overcome such sorrows, pains, and miseries just like Jesus. Even if you have become a victor by fighting centered on personal pain, personal sorrow, and personal misery for personal restoration, you cannot transcend to the family era.

That is why those born in the end times are blessed. To develop from the individual era to the family, tribe, nation, and global era, there must be historical sorrow, historical pain, and historical misery involved. If you participate in global misery, global pain, and global sorrow, you will stand in a place that has passed through historical sorrow, pain, and misery.

Then how does God govern? In personal providence centered on the individual, He places one individual in a position of misery, pain, and sorrow to overcome it. If you follow him, God will also grant you the value of having overcome it.

In Moses' time, God placed Moses in a position of misery, sorrow, and pain. If at that time the Israelite people had followed him, they could have overcome national misery, sorrow, and pain. When Jesus was placed in the position of sorrow, pain, and misery of the cross, if they had followed him, they could have overcome global misery, sorrow, and pain. If they had followed him in joy, in sorrow, and even in death, they would have overcome global misery, sorrow, and pain. The Gospel until now has been to alleviate the global historical sorrow, pain, and misery so that humanity can follow Jesus and participate in the providence of salvation.

Preparation to Become a Victorious Subject
In light of this, what will happen in the end times? If the Christians scattered throughout the world can achieve victory from the place of 6,000 years of end-time sorrow, pain, and misery, the coming Lord will have nothing to do with sorrow, pain, and misery. However, if the Christians scattered throughout the world fail to lay such a foundation, the coming Lord will inevitably experience sorrow, pain, and misery on behalf of the saints. This is similar to how Jesus had to taste sorrow, pain, and misery due to the failure of the Jewish nation that God had established. You must understand this.

If you have been called in a place where the conditions of indemnity and restoration have been established, you must obey absolutely. Until when must you obey absolutely? You must obey absolutely until you establish one sovereignty and mobilize one nation and one people to strike down the fallen lifestyle. How long did the Israelite people have to obey Moses' command? They had to obey absolutely until they destroyed the seven tribes of Canaan. Noah's family also had to obey Noah absolutely. Until when did they have to obey? They had to obey absolutely for three generations, that is, until the grandchildren's time.

You too must follow absolutely when that time comes. Only then will you establish the condition that you have overcome the sorrows, pains, and miseries of the era. Otherwise, you cannot transcend.

What I am asking you this morning is to become victorious subjects. The term victorious subject is very good. However, it is extremely difficult to embody its content. You must understand that there is a bloody struggle involved in this. Therefore, you must break through the highest standards of sorrow, the highest standards of pain, and the highest standards of misery. Even if you enter a place where you are beaten and bleed, you must pray for blessings for your enemies. Why? Because even enemies, having faith, hope, and love, can eventually be brought to a position where they can be restored after passing through a certain time.

So, what kind of determination must you have to become such victorious subjects? A global historical era is approaching us, and you must not separate this from yourselves. Family sorrow is sorrow, but if there is national sorrow, you must take that as your sorrow and be determined to take responsibility for it. If there is global sorrow, you must also take that as your sorrow and be determined to take responsibility for it. 

The same goes for pain. Individual pain and family pain are pain, but if there is national pain, you must recognize it as your pain and be determined to take responsibility for it.

Until you resolve this, even in a position where you have something, it is still pain, and even in a position where you can give to others, it is still pain. Until all of humanity can face the global purpose entity and see him as the object of hope, faith, and love, the sorrows, pains, and miseries will remain. You must critically evaluate this issue.

Moreover, 1964 is not a good year numerically. Therefore, even if you suffer this year, you must approach it with the attitude that you are experiencing historical pain, historical misery, and historical sorrow. You must resolve to complete everything with this mindset. This is the resolution that must be made in 1964.

The Path of Indemnity and Restoration to Walk Alone
To achieve this, you must have the patience to prepare for it. To endure everything, you need the strength to overcome it. So, what should be the motivation for that patience? It is the understanding that I am the son or daughter of the Father, that I must go together with the Father, and that if I do not go, the Father will go and then return to take me with Him. If I sit down here, the Father will have to come back after going and take me again.

If we cannot go at once, we must go through it three times. You must understand that by being crucified, Jesus went to the cross, came back to the cross, and then returned again. If such things do not happen at the individual level, they will happen at the family level. If it is not resolved there, it will happen at the family level. Otherwise, heaven will go and then come back to go again. This principle applies to the nation, state, and world as well. This is the bond between father and child. We must go together.
There is a sorrow in rock, and if we do not go together, we must understand that humanity must endure all pain and sadness alone. Considering God's position in this matter, we must follow with a humble and apologetic heart, laboring through great hardships. When you are unable to walk the path you should take, the Father walks that path in sorrow, and you must understand that He returns in sorrow after having walked it in sorrow. 

If we move in sorrow and advance with God, He will look upon us and find comfort, have hope, and feel greater indignation against the enemy. If we do not move in such a way, God will feel more pain than hope when He looks upon us, and more pain than indignation against the enemy. When thinking about this, you must realize that you are causing pain to God, who knows the steps you should take.

No matter what pain and sorrow may come, and no matter how miserable the situation may be, you must understand that the one who comes to drive those things away is your Father. In such situations, you should worry about whether anyone will sympathize with you. You should not seek support from a third party. Fundamentally, it is just the Father and you. If you receive support from a third party, what happens? When you go to the other world, if that person is in a more glorious position than you, it may be fine, but if they are not, you will have to take responsibility for that person.

Thus, the path of indemnity and restoration is never a path taken with support. It is a path that does not receive support from angels, nor from comrades; it is a path taken alone. Noah went alone, Abraham went alone, Moses went alone, and Jesus went alone. You must understand that even though they have paved the way, there is still a sorrow that needs to be restored.

Unification Church members must advance toward the saddest place of this era. Because there are many such hurdles remaining, patience is required to overcome them. The question is how to cultivate this patience. Now that you know the path you must take, you must also understand how much you have caused God to suffer. Who would have thought that Moses striking the rock twice could lead to Jesus being crucified? The path to heaven is one that requires perseverance, even when you want to express your anger, and you must walk it while quietly receiving the attacks of evil, avoiding direct confrontation. The teacher has walked such a path.

Now we have entered an era where we can face tribes and nations from the personal era. God has established democracy so that you can walk the heavenly path centered on the global environment. You do not know how blessed this is. It is now time for you to go freely toward the world. However, the ultimate issue is not the world but the nation. The problem is with the nation and the people. This is the ultimate issue. Once this is resolved, the world will not be a problem. The path to the world will open up at once.

If, during Jesus' time, the nation of Israel and Judaism had united around Jesus to form a global sovereign state, Christianity would not have become what it is today. Christianity might not have even existed. Moreover, the world would have already become one. However, because such a standard was not established, countless people have walked the miserable, sad, and painful path that Jesus walked for two thousand years. Knowing this, you must have patience.

I have seen people suffering in prisons, shackled and in pain, and I thought about how blessed it would be if they could walk with God while enduring such suffering for a purpose. Have you ever thought about this? Have you ever thought that it is okay to suffer so miserably for the purpose? If such a path still remains, what will you do? If you cannot go, God must go.

Every time you see the world's misery, sadness, or pain, you must have a heart that feels it is not someone else's but your own responsibility. You should also have the desire to treat humanity with tears, blood, and sweat. Only then, even if you cannot actually carry out such actions, can you stand in a position where your heart and actions become one through tears and blood, thus carrying the condition of having acted in reality.

Then, what responsibilities do you, as Unification Church members, have for the nation and the state in relation to the world? You must advance toward the saddest place of this era. You must go to the most painful place. Going to the saddest place is the way to live, and going to the most painful place is the way to live. You must know how to go for the purpose even in a situation where your own child is starving to death. If you go out with the heart to take responsibility for that, fearing that it might be a shame before God, the fate of this nation will change. The misery of this nation will also disappear.

We must take the shortest path to become victorious subjects. So how do we take the shortest path? It is by walking the path of the greatest sorrow, pain, and misery mentioned earlier. This path must be overcome with patience. It must be overcome without fail. If this path is not overcome, what will happen? You must understand that God suffers the sorrow of having to come and go again, and that He suffers more than three times the pain because of you. And you must stand in a position where you feel an unending sense of shame for not being able to fulfill the responsibilities imposed on you in this era, even with the debts you have incurred until now.

Now we must feel all the sorrow of this nation! We must feel all the pain of this nation. We must claim all the misery of this nation as our own. If we do this, we will never perish. God will also be with us.

The attitude for the four-year course
Then how long will this period be? Everything is accomplished according to principled numbers. Therefore, we must indemnify the pain, sorrow, and misery of this nation within four years. Thus, when praying to the Father, you should pray, "Please make me someone who can endure and survive in sorrow, pain, and misery, and allow me to be a child of God who can set up an altar before God by managing that miserable environment."

If you are a Unification Church that can kneel down and sincerely report the facts and pray for blessings while sweating and shedding blood every day, just wait for four years. **<Message>** The title I wish to speak about today is the Path of Restoration. The Path of Restoration. The noun "restoration" is not a joyful noun for us.  
Because humanity has fallen, the noun "salvation" has become necessary, and because we are in a position that requires salvation, the noun "restoration" has become necessary. We know well that humanity has fallen into death because of sin.
We also know that a Messiah, that is, a Savior, is needed to save such humanity. If the ancestor of humanity had not fallen, terms like salvation, restoration, and Lord would have had nothing to do with us. However, we understand that because of the fall, terms like salvation, restoration, and Lord have come into existence.

**The Purpose of Human Fall and Restoration**
Originally, when God created humans, He made them as the embodiment of His hope and as the representation of His heart. However, due to the fall, God's hope, ideals, and heart have vanished without a trace, and today on this earth, only the hope and heart of the satanic world remain. Therefore, all things that exist were created by God but have ended up existing in the embrace of an unwilling enemy.

God created humans to be the embodiment that could represent His inner heart, but due to the fall, their existence has become one of sorrow before God, symbolizing regret and resentment. However, we know that God cannot simply abandon such humans who harbor resentment. This is because He created all things centered on His will and principles. As long as the heart of the Father remains, He cannot fundamentally destroy the created beings and humans. If He were to destroy all things and humans, He would have to endure a greater pain than that which He felt when establishing His will and heart. Therefore, God seeks to find beings and people who can be restored to His original will and heart in this world and humanity.

In restoration, while it is important to restore each individual human, it is even more crucial to restore all fallen humanity to its original position, which has not fallen. Furthermore, we must understand that unless we return all things that have departed from God's embrace and are now in the enemy's embrace back to God, the purpose of restoration will not be fulfilled. If the purpose of restoration is not achieved, there will be no hope, ideals, or glory for God, and He will not be able to enjoy happiness with the created beings made with His heart.

**The Path of Restoration**
Therefore, God's providence of salvation aims to fulfill His will and to find children who can connect with His heart, to create a world of happiness, an eternal foundation of unchanging glory, and to rejoice and enjoy with all of creation on the foundation of life, love, and victory, ultimately achieving eternal life in heaven. We must understand that only by creating such a heavenly environment can God find the purpose of creation He desires, and it is with this goal that we carry out the history of restoration.

**The Content of Restoration and Human Ignorance**
So how should restoration be carried out? As we know through principles, it must begin with the restoration of all things. Therefore, we are moving from the age of offerings in the Old Testament to the age of the Word in the New Testament, and then into the age of reality.

In the process of restoring from the age of offerings to the age of reality, from which position must we humans begin to restore? From the day the ancestor of humanity received the lineage of Satan, humanity has been tied to Satan by an inseparable bloodline and has become children of the enemy, unable to turn back before God.

However, God is leading humans, born as children of Satan, into a position where they cannot receive Satan's love, pulling them toward His side. God has been working from the age of servants to the age of adopted children, then to the age of true daughters, and finally to the age of true parents. Thus, God is carrying out a history of rising up in reverse.

If humans had not fallen, we would not need terms like servant or adopted child. We would have become the forms acknowledged by God and advanced to the position of true parents in the eternal garden of God's goodness, centered on God's love. We must understand that God's providence of salvation and the history of restoration is to elevate us from the status of servants and adopted children to become sons and daughters, receiving the love of the Father and advancing to the position of true couples.

When we compare God, who is carrying out this history, with the ancestors of humanity who have faced this history and the humans of the present age, we find that many people living on this earth today do not know that God is carrying out the history of restoration. They are also unaware that our ancestors made great efforts to pave the way for restoration, and in the course of that effort, they swore loyalty to God but later broke that vow, causing sorrow to God.

We must understand that it is not possible to restore such humans all at once due to the complexities of heaven. Because the ancestor of humanity made a mistake and turned the world upside down, a central figure is needed to restore the fall of Adam and Eve. Thus, we know that God has wandered for 6,000 years to find a central figure who can become the true ancestor of humanity. We also understand that before establishing this central figure, God has been preparing an external foundation that can support this central figure, carrying out a long providential history for 6,000 years up to today.

However, today, Christians scattered around the world do not realize the greatness of their mission. It is similar to how the Israelite people, chosen as a holy nation through 4,000 years of history, failed to fulfill their responsibilities and mission as a chosen people. The Israelite people were supposed to bear the responsibility of God's will along with the Messiah sent by God, but because they could not unite with Him, history became entangled, and the Israelite people, whom God sought, fell into the world of death, while the Messiah, who was to establish God's will, died on the cross. Therefore, God is gathering the Second Israel to establish the Third Israel to restore a new global Canaan on this earth.

From this perspective, when we consider that we must fulfill the mission of restoration, and compare God, our ancestors, and ourselves, we must recognize that this era is neither the First Israel era nor the Second Israel era, but rather the Third Israel era moving toward the global restoration of Canaan. We must understand that this is a critical time when we must engage in fierce struggles to raise the banner of victory and move forward with heaven's command.

**The Restoration Providence Centered on Jacob**
God, who is carrying out the providence of restoration, could not restore heaven and earth all at once, so He began with individuals. To establish one individual, God chose Jacob 4,000 years ago and worked to transition from the age of the servant of servants to the age of servants. He worked to settle the era before Jacob, who could not be called a servant of God, and to move into the age of servants.

However, to escape the age of the servant of servants, one must lay a foundation of victory by obeying God's command. Only then can one move from being a servant individual to a servant family and then to a servant nation.

What was the purpose of the 4,000 years of history before the coming of Jesus? It was a history of struggles to expand from the individual of the servant to the family of the servant and then to establish a nation of servants to subdue the enemy, Satan. We must recognize that this history was a struggle to lay the foundation for restoring the age of servants. To lay the foundation for personal victory, Jacob had to go through a process of personal struggle. In this position, Jacob received the cooperation of his mother. We know well that Jacob, knowing that his father was about to bless Esau, acted according to his mother's instructions and took away the birthright.

Having received this blessing and standing on the foundation of personal victory, Jacob passed through the wilderness of Haran and went to Laban's house. However, even though he laid a foundation of personal victory, Jacob had to establish a family foundation before God to make a national start. Thus, Jacob, unable to make a national start directly, went to Laban's house and laid a family foundation for 21 years.

Even in a miserable living environment, he longed only for God and deeply missed his homeland. We must understand that Jacob, despite being deceived by Laban, remained loyal to God for 21 years. God blessed Jacob, took away everything in Laban's household, and allowed him to return to Canaan with a new victorious family foundation.

What was to happen next for Jacob's family? Jacob's family had to go to the battlefield on behalf of the nation. Because of this destiny, Jacob's 70 family members went to the land of Egypt.

**Moses' Love for the Nation**
During the 400 years when the Israelite people disappeared as miserable offerings under the cruel hand of Pharaoh, they were subjected to the tyrannical rule of Pharaoh, who was busy sucking their blood and flesh. This period of 400 years of suffering in Egypt was a time of exhaustion, despair, and the potential loss of their national identity.

However, the more severe the trials faced by the Israelite people, the greater the hope that surged within their hearts. That hope was that they were the blessed people of Israel. This sentiment did not change, regardless of the trials and adversities they faced. Because of this heart, they did not tire in their national struggles and longed for God, and their deep patriotism for the blessed nation of Israel cried out. We must understand that it was with this heart that God raised up Moses to lead them.

Moses, after failing in his first plan to establish his will in the royal palace of Pharaoh for 40 years, prayed countless times while thinking of the return to Canaan. He knew that the Israelite people were a blessed nation and that they were descendants of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob. Therefore, he believed that the Israelite people should not be toyed with by the enemy, Satan.

Moses earnestly anticipated the day of returning to Canaan, even in the luxurious palace of Pharaoh. He never ceased to pray, longing for his homeland. We must recognize this about Moses. The more he felt the great suffering and pain of the Israelite people while living in luxury, the more he was compelled to love the Israelite people.

During his 40 years of shepherding in the wilderness of Midian, every time he led the flock, he did not forget the Israelite people who were groaning under Pharaoh's rule in Egypt. Every time he gathered the flock, he felt a surge of conviction on behalf of the Israelite people. In such circumstances, he prayed, "O living God! Do not forsake Israel."

Though the Israelite people did not know Moses, we must understand that he lived in such a way in the wilderness of Midian that God could not help but remember him. Moses did not tire during the long trials of 40 years, nor did he become a dropout in any harsh environment. His only desire was to lead the Israelite people centered on God's desired will. Therefore, God finally called Moses and sent him before the Israelite people.

Moses, knowing that God's will was his will and that his will was the will of the Israelite people, never thought of betraying God, even in his dreams. He never entertained the thought of betraying the Israelite people. Even if heaven and earth were to change, his heart toward the Israelite people could not change. With this heart, the path Moses walked was the path God walked, and it was the path the Israelite people had to walk.

From this perspective, we know that Moses led the Israelite people and fought against Pharaoh multiple times, ultimately subduing the Egyptian people and laying the foundation for national victory as they set out toward the land of Canaan.

The Israelite people, having left Egypt, understood that whether they lived or died in the wilderness, their wish was Moses' wish, and Moses' wish was God's wish. They had to keep in mind that as long as Moses did not forsake God, God would not forsake them either. This was the mission of Israel.

**The Reason the Israelite People Fell in the Wilderness**
God allowed them to go through trials for 400 years to construct a new Canaan kingdom. 

Then why did the Israelite people, who did not fall during their suffering in Egypt, fall in the wilderness? When God raised Moses to lead the Israelite people, they believed that from the day they received Moses' guidance, everything would go smoothly, and the world would align with their wishes. However, the path of restoration does not work that way.

To find an individual, one must go through personal struggles; to find a family, one must go through family struggles; to find a nation, one must go through national struggles; to find a country, one must go through national struggles; and to find heaven on earth, one must go through a heavenly struggle. The Israelite people did not understand this.

When God stood on the side of Israel and brought down the ten plagues, the Israelite people thought they could command the world. God had established the Israelite people to build a nation, but they did not fulfill their responsibilities and only wanted to stand in the position of those who had completed their duties. The Israelite people, unaware that they had to fulfill their mission and responsibilities, complained when their path was not smooth, and the more difficult their journey became, the more discontent they expressed. The Israelite people, who did not understand God's will in calling them and raising Moses to lead them, could not overcome the trials they faced on their journey and fell into despair. This became the trigger for the 600,000 Israelites to become food for the eagles in the wilderness.

Originally, after the Israelite people achieved national victory, they were to enter the land of Canaan and drive out the seven nations of Canaan. This was the path the Israelite people had to take. The purpose of establishing King Saul was to create a sovereign nation to strike against the nations of the satanic world. Just as God struck down the firstborn in Egypt, His command to Saul was to strike down and conquer all that belonged to the satanic world. Despite having a great mission and responsibilities, King Saul betrayed God's will by thinking from a human and personal perspective. As a result, the ideal of the temple that God intended to establish during Saul's reign was extended to King David and King Solomon. This temple ideal was originally to have been achieved by Moses without falling in the wilderness.
