Father and His Kingdom
The title I want to talk to you about today is "The Father and His Kingdom." I will speak for a moment under this title.

The purpose of God in creating heaven and earth
Every object created by humans in this world has an owner. And that object has the purpose of the owner who created it, and the object itself has its own purpose. 

We also know that there is a creator of heaven and earth. We call the creator of this universe God. However, all things created by God are not with God, and the world created by God has become a fallen world. Since the day of the fall, all things have lost their owner. Thus, all things are in a position where they must find their lost owner and re-establish a relationship. We know that the path of restoration is the way to find the lost owner.

So what purpose did the owner who created heaven and earth have? The owner created all things to be the center of hope that can appear through humans, to be a Father to humanity. These created things should have been able to be loved by their owner and to love their owner. They should have become God's things, belonging to God's kingdom. However, they could not become so, and heaven was separated from heaven, earth from earth, and humans from humans. We know this is the fall.

That is why God has come to restore this separation. While restoring heaven and earth, He has come to restore everything centered on humanity. This is the path of restoration that God has walked.

Originally, God and we humans had a relationship that could not be forgotten eternally, a relationship that could not be severed. However, due to the fall of humanity, God could not stand in the position of our Father, and we humans could not stand in the position of God's children. If there is the most pitiful person in this world, who would that person be? It would be someone who cannot call their child their child, someone who cannot call their parent their parent. There is no one more pitiful than that. Furthermore, if a husband and wife have made a vow and established a relationship but cannot love each other, who could be more pitiful than that?

Restoring the relationship between God and humanity
What position are God and we humans in today? God is our Father, and we humans are His children, yet we are in a position where we cannot be so. The original relationship between God and humanity is that of a parent and child, which is the core thought of Christianity. Moreover, this is also the fundamental content of the creation of heaven and earth.

Therefore, humans must go to a position where they can establish a parent-child relationship with God. What could be more miserable and sad than the world that has become one where the relationship between God (Father) and humanity (sons and daughters) has been severed? Thus, it is natural for God to be sad, but we humans, who have lost God, are also in a position where we should be sad. We must understand that there is no greater sorrow than the earth that has lost the heaven that should be received as a bride.

So, if there is something we must seek with all of heaven and earth, what would that be? It is to find the lost Father, to find the lost children, and to find the lost bride and groom. The path to seek these things is the path of restoration. On this path of restoration, God has asked, "Have you ever had a day when you could say, 'I am God'?" You have not had that day. Although God created the world for His beloved sons and daughters, He could not say, "This is my kingdom." Have many people who believe in God ever said that this world is mine? They have not.

Thus, this world has become a world that has lost its owner. So what has become the owner of this world instead of God? It is Satan, the enemy of God and our enemy, who has become the owner. All things have become those who have lost their rightful owner, and humanity has become those who have lost their original parents. When we think of the universe and humanity that have lost their owners and parents, what must we do? We must find the lost parents and repay the unpardonable enmity of the parents. We must keep in mind that this is our duty as humans.

What is the path of restoration for? It is to find the lost Father and the kingdom centered on that Father. To achieve this, we must receive God's blessing as victorious sons and daughters, going through the positions of servant, adopted child, and child. Then, centered on God, we must become true parents, create families, build tribes, form nations, and establish the world. This is the purpose of restoration that God desires.

Has there ever been a time when God has raised an individual and said, "I am surely your Father, and you are surely my son"? There has not been such a person. God sent Jesus to this earth and said, "This is my beloved Son." He called him His only begotten Son. However, even though He sent His beloved Son and only begotten Son to this earth, God could not love him to the end. For the first time since creation, God could not love the Messiah who had the title of His beloved only begotten Son. What greater grievance could there be than this? It is the same for God, but what about Jesus, who was sent? 

"Father! Please love me," He could not even say. All He could say was, "My Father! If it is possible, let this cup pass from me" (Matthew 26:39). This statement carries great meaning. Although He should have received the Father's love, there were conditions and limitations that prevented Him from receiving it freely. It was a love that could only be looked upon, a love that could only be longed for, a love that could only be awaited. Therefore, He could not say, "My Father!" or "My Son!"

Many believers in Jesus on this earth claim to be God's sons and daughters. But is there anyone who truly has the heart of a son or daughter burning with the passionate love that comes from God's heart? Is there anyone whom God can say, "Yes, you are my son," and embrace with open arms? There is not. The universe remains as it is, and while there are many people in human form, there is no one who can govern the universe. There is no one who can monopolize God's love.

God, who has borne the responsibility of restoration and has come forth in providence
Even Jesus, who has gone to heaven, must pray. The Holy Spirit must also labor in childbirth. Why must this be so? It is because there remains a grievance that must be indemnified due to the fall. We must resolve the grievances that are bound from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, world, and the heavenly and earthly realms. Without resolving these grievances, heaven and earth cannot establish a relationship. Heaven is the bridegroom, and the earth is the bride. God is the parent of humanity, and humanity is the children of God. We must establish this relationship.

So what exactly is this Satan, or this devil? He is a thief who has stolen the love that can never be separated between heaven and earth, God and humanity. Until we receive surrender from this Satan, we cannot prevent the destruction of the family.

Today, the fallen descendants are unconsciously heading towards heaven, following what their true hearts desire. They are moving forward even while falling and stumbling. They have gone through a history of falling and stumbling, both individually, nationally, and globally. However, what is commendable among all this is that even though they have lost God and have gone through countless stumbles, the name of God has remained in the hearts of humanity until now. The fact that even the name of God remains is a blessing. Moreover, it is a blessing that the name of Jesus remains, even though He has gone. However, while you pray in the name of Jesus, I have never prayed that way from the beginning. I do not pray in the name of Jesus.

Throughout the historical journey, there have been many twists and turns, but as we have come to this day, we can now call heaven the bridegroom and earth the bride, we can call Jesus the bridegroom, and we can call the Holy Spirit the bride. We can call God our Father and humanity His children. We must recognize that this teaching, this terminology, is being spread in this complicated world and is establishing a global stage. You may think that all of this has come about because of the evangelism of Christians up to now. Of course, it is true that many Christians have sacrificed themselves from a sacrificial standpoint, but more than that, it is because God, who is behind them, has allowed His name to remain and has allowed the standard He desires to be established among humans on this earth.
came to be in a position where he had to bear the cross alone. This is the path that God has walked, and you must understand that this is the way God has come to find you.

To qualify as children and brides before God, today’s leaders representing this era must first overcome the trials of their tribes. Only then can they move their tribes into the realm of nations. Just as Moses had to endure trials within the nation to guide the Israelites, he also had to overcome national trials in the Midian wilderness to establish a foundation for victory. Only on that foundation can a leader guide their people without being slandered.

God, who leads ignorant humans, is enduring trials and tribulations greater than those faced by humanity to prevent our destruction. While we endure trials within the familial or national realms, God is busy establishing a foundation that is national and global. We must understand this.

Until now, many who have approached God have not known this truth; they have only appealed to God about their own sorrows. They have cried out, “Father, please accept my tears.” Those who claim to be God’s faithful sons and daughters have acted this way until now. They must realize that their personal crosses are not due to their own faults but are meant to replace the familial crosses on a global scale. After overcoming their own crosses, they should be able to say, “Father! I have laid the foundation for familial victory, so please grant me the national cross.”

However, many of you wish to keep blessings for yourselves while placing all difficulties on God. This is a selfish mindset. You must understand this clearly.

When I interact with you, I sometimes say that God walks one world ahead of humanity. Because God walks ahead, while we are trying to establish families, God is preparing a national foundation. When we are in the process of overcoming national trials, God is walking the overwhelming path of the cross to expand the national and global foundations. We, as members of the Unification Church, must not forget this.

Today, we are to be God’s sons and daughters who support Him, and brides who support the Bridegroom. Have we truly lived this way? We must reflect on this again. The Father and His Kingdom: The Father is our Father, and the Kingdom is our Kingdom. Yet, due to humanity, the Father has become so miserable, and His Kingdom has gone astray. God bears the cross that humanity alone should bear, and He walks the path of suffering that humanity should walk. Until you feel this deep sense of grievance, you cannot truly become beloved sons and daughters of God, nor can you qualify as brides before the Bridegroom.

When I observe the ignorant hearts of Unification Church members in the provinces, I think about how God feels when He looks at the Unification Church. We must remember that God is ahead of us, carrying the cross to pave our way. We should encourage Him by saying, “Let’s go!” and devote all our strength to fulfilling our responsibilities before God.

Today, we must become faithful sons and daughters. We must become loyal subjects and virtuous women. In what situations can we receive the titles of faithful sons and daughters, loyal subjects, and virtuous women? Only on the path of the cross can we receive these titles. Jesus also received His title only at the place where He exchanged His life on the path of the cross. You must understand this clearly. Can you claim to be God’s sons and daughters without walking this path? Can you claim to be the Bride of Jesus? Such desires are too selfish.

When we move toward the path of the cross, everything will be fulfilled. The titles of faithful son, faithful daughter, loyal subject, and virtuous woman cannot be received on smooth paths. This is because God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit are striving ahead of us to pave the way of faith. We are the saints who must bear the painful mission. Can God, who must watch the saints who are dying, be at peace? Can God, who cannot tell Jesus, who is suffering, to resist that pain, be at ease? We must understand that as we encounter trials, persecutions, and tribulations, the burden of God’s cross also increases proportionately.

Therefore, to become the sons and daughters of God, we must walk the path of the cross. God is walking the path of hunger. When have you ever devoted your sincerity for such a God? When there was something good, you stole it all for yourself. The path to God is not for eating, not for playing, and certainly not for comfort. To become a true servant who can host the true Master (God), you must abandon your decaying body and receive the title of a true servant. If you have a parent to serve, you must receive the title of “my beloved son or daughter” even in the most difficult situations. If there is a king to serve, you must receive the title of a loyal subject even in the most difficult circumstances. Only then can you become a being that cannot be occupied by the enemy, Satan. Once you become such a being, you will never lose God again. You will become a faithful son, a loyal subject, and a virtuous woman before God.

So, in what situation will God seek true sons and daughters? It is on the path of the cross. Ultimately, He calls us on the path of the cross. To follow that Father, we must establish a connection on the path of the cross and receive the title of “my beloved son or daughter.” But does that mean everything will work out? Not at all.

Alongside the personal cross, there is also a familial cross. Therefore, Jacob, after successfully crossing the personal cross before Esau, sought the path of the familial cross. After winning on the path of the familial cross, he must go to the path of the national cross. Then, he must proceed to the path of the national cross. That is why Moses went to the land of Canaan to find the nation, the land of Israel, through the path of the cross. However, because the Israelites failed to take responsibility on this path of the cross, the conditions were established for Jesus to be crucified later.

Based on the foundation of victory on the path of the national and state crosses, it was the mission of the Messiah who came to this earth to pioneer the path of the global cross. Therefore, even though the Jewish nation, the Israelite people, and the Jews should have believed in the Messiah who was coming, they failed to fulfill their mission, causing Jesus to lose his national and state foundation. Consequently, Jesus fell from the position of a king to a position lower than that of Moses and Jacob. The Israelite people, who had been prepared for 4,000 years, betrayed Him on a national basis, causing Jesus to leave his family, tribe, and nation and go into the wilderness. Drawn by Satan into the wilderness, Jesus had to fight against him.
God has once again sought the foundation of 4,000 years, which has been established through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and in a national context. Through spiritual battles, we have forged the basis for victory. This is the path of restoration.

In this era of restoration, our Unification Church is now looking toward a four-year course. Rather than praying about how to walk this four-year course, you should pray about how to prepare for the course after the four years. I believe the four-year course will go well, and a wise person is one who seeks the path to take after four years.

The purpose of our lives
You have come this far without falling on the path of evil persecution and have remained among the survivors. You have not died in the crowd. Why? Because you knew that God was guiding us. Can you stop God's footsteps? When you try to halt His steps, they only become faster. Isn't that so? They become faster. If you collapse under your personal cross, you cannot surpass the standard of the family cross. If you fall on the path of the family cross, you cannot surpass the tribal, national, and state standards.

Today, we must develop a global standard centered on the four-year course and based on the standards of our nation and people. The question is how to break through to a position where we can become loyal subjects and virtuous women before God on this global Golgotha. God is advancing beyond the limitations of this era. When we take responsibility for the national era, God prepares for the global era, and when we take responsibility for the global era, God prepares for the heavenly era. So, which cross is heavier, the one we bear or God's? It is God’s that is heavier.

Now, what must we do? When God leads our path from the mountain of the cross, we must go that way and become victors, becoming those whom God can save. We must continue until we hear the voice saying that victory is all that remains for you. What stage are you currently at? You must think carefully.

When considering these things, although you are sitting here now, God has no rest. Today, the Unification Church is not the problem. Korea is not the problem. Moreover, the teacher is not the problem. Everything in history is at stake.

You must feel yourself in such a time. Nowadays, it seems that nothing has changed from the past. Although there is still the path of the cross to walk, you are not going.

The purpose for which I have walked is to find the Father, and the purpose of my life is to restore the Father's kingdom. Since the Father is weeping, I cannot live comfortably; since the Father is worried, I cannot rest easily; since the Father is bearing the cross, I cannot be in a comfortable position.

We must conquer the cross
When considering this meaning, the current situation in Korea is very urgent. The global situation is becoming more urgent the more we look at it. What kind of group can take responsibility on behalf of God at the peak of the global cross? The time has come when we must think about such things. Those who dislike this path and turn away are following the group that betrayed Jesus, who bore the cross.

Today, our Korean people must have the conviction that we must save the many nations of the world with our own hands. We must have the conviction that we cannot yield this mission to other nations. Furthermore, Unification Church believers must have the conviction that it must be the Unification Church that saves this nation and this people. We must be the first to bear the difficult cross. As God bears the cross in a starving position, we too must bear the cross and resolve to go without food. This is what it means to be a loyal child. Even in a starving position, we must have the desire to give and offer. 

We must do this. This is what I must do. 
If God is in a thirsty position, I must also bear the cross in that same position. I must learn to carry the path of the cross that God must walk in a thirsty position and to hand over what is comfortable to God. Even if I become a weary traveler who can no longer rest, I must be able to say before God, "I am okay." I must not attach my situation to God but stand in a position to relieve God's burden through myself.

From this standpoint, I must recognize the cross I bear as my responsibility, knowing that God bears a greater cross than I do, and become someone who can give, care for, and serve. Such a person is a true loyal child.

Then, for whom does God carry out His providence? Beyond families, it is for nations. It is for something greater than that. God, who bears the national responsibility from the perspective of the nation, does not take lightly even the smallest person who can fulfill any responsibility within that national realm. 

You must become someone who has a compassionate heart like God and step forward to alleviate the suffering of the cross that God endures. God will accept all actions of such a person as being done for Himself.

Today, Unification Church members must bear the family cross and add the national cross to it. This is the attitude of Unification Church members. Even if you fail at the family altar, you can leave behind the title of loyal subject from the national perspective and the title of loyal child. When considering this, we realize that our Unification Church has entered an era where it must fulfill its national mission. Now, looking at the four-year course, the path we must take is a global path, and the country we must seek is the heavenly land. We must think about how great the remaining path of the cross is until we can present this heavenly land to God. Therefore, the cross we bear now is only natural.

If you stop your steps here, you will become someone who simply paves the way and then just leaves. In the Unification Church, we will connect the stages of the rebirth era, growth era, and completion era step by step. Therefore, what you must remember once again is that in this era, you must keep your spirit straight and run the remaining path of the cross.

Every time you encounter trials on the path of the cross, you must pray, "Thank you." When walking the path of the cross, you must hold onto not only the national cross but also the global cross. Only by conquering the cross can you overcome the trials of the satanic world. Jesus was able to establish a new history of resurrection and begin the history of the New Testament gospel after conquering the cross.

In the same way, today, we Unification Church members must conquer the cross. We must conquer the cross of this world. Thus, we must become a group that does not perish even when facing trials and persecutions. This is how God guides us. Because this path of restoration remains, whenever you feel that your situation is lonely and miserable, you must think of God's position, who walks with you.

You may rest, but God is laboring.
John the Baptist said about Jesus, "Behold, the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world." (John 1:29) This is true. The Lamb of God who bears the cross of the world must break through all the peaks of the cross that permeate from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world, and beyond to the heavenly land and the cosmos. We must break through the Golgotha of the spirit world and the Golgotha of the earthly world. Therefore, we must overcome the peaks of the personal cross, the family cross, and the national, tribal, and global crosses.

You must choose to do the most difficult tasks. When you encounter the most difficult challenges, you must say, "Teacher, I will do it. I will try it once." You must strive to bear the cross even to the point of God's cross. In this journey where you must bear the heavenly mission, what responsibilities and missions are you carrying as you cross the difficult peaks? Everything must be done with God as the focus. The reason you are hungry is not because you cannot eat. You are not thirsty because you cannot drink. You may say various things, but can those words accomplish anything? Matters concerning life cannot be resolved with words. Whatever you say will only last for that moment. 

We must bear a great cross. Personal trials and family trials were a preparation period for laying the foundation for the tribe. Now, do not think that the absence of persecution and trials before us means that our path will be smooth. The scope has now widened. In the past, we bore the cross while sitting, but now we must walk while bearing the cross. In the past, we only looked in one direction while bearing the cross, but now we must not only look in one direction. We must look to the east, west, north, and south as we go. In the past, we could ascend the peak of the cross from that position, but now we must look around and be vigilant as we go. The scope has expanded.

The teacher must uphold the path that God walks, and you must uphold the path that the teacher walks. You must stand in the same position. You must not be disconnected from each other. The Unification Church teacher walks a path that is heavier than yours. Moreover, the God who guides the teacher walks a path that is even higher. Even if you are asleep, God has gone through the three stages of rebirth, growth, and completion to establish a relationship.

Just as one is judged in the growth stage after passing through the rebirth stage, the second is the problem. The second is the issue. There is a hierarchy, and there are front and back, left and right, all because of the second. The responsibility to correct the hierarchy and the front and back, left and right, lies with the second.

Recently, when I hear news from the Japanese church, I learn that high school students in Japan all come to church after finishing their studies at school. They leave their backpacks at church and go out to evangelize, each one evangelizing and then returning home. This movement is happening. What have the adults and youth here been doing until now? Even if you do not move, God does not rest. If you do not do it, I will.

Looking toward the final battle, only those who take responsibility can return alive. Since the path is so long that it cannot be completed in a lifetime, you must be awake even in your dreams. Are you in that state? Do you only wish for comfort? You must not do that. You must be dignified no matter what hardships come when you take on public responsibilities. You must become a shield for the Lord, who bears the cross, even while carrying the fence of the environment you must go through, rather than placing the burden on the Lord. Public missions and personal responsibilities are different.

Let us become those who establish the Father's kingdom
The teacher thought about how he could walk the path that God is concerned about, even if it meant collapsing from hunger and exhaustion. He thought about how he could walk the path of the cross that he could bear. However, you are not preparing to walk this path. Today, you know that you are saved through service, yet you look on shamelessly. You must not stop with such a mindset.

We must go out for the Father and for the Father's kingdom, even if it means dying a thousand or ten thousand times. If you have such courage, you must be able to bear your own cross and take on God's cross.

That is why today we must work for the Father and His kingdom. We must become loyal children whom the Father can call. Men must become loyal sons of the Father, and women must become loyal daughters of the Father. We must become loyal subjects and virtuous women before the Father. We must clearly recognize that we are a people destined to serve God, loyal children, loyal sons and daughters, and virtuous women. This is our mission.

The path our Unification Church walks is difficult. Even on the difficult path of the cross, we must say, "Father, not my will, but Yours be done." Is it the Father's will for us to bleed and collapse? Is it the Father's will for us to suffer? It is because we must repay the Father's enemies that we can only do it this way. It cannot be done otherwise.

Knowing this, we must become sons and daughters who serve the Father and become loyal subjects and virtuous women. We are going forth to meet that day when we can do so. We must become a group of the Unification Church that is determined to be victors and not losers on this path. Now, let us work hard to the point of exhaustion.

To become loyal children before the Father and loyal subjects and virtuous women before the kingdom, we must be able to bear the crosses of our parents and siblings and the crosses of our people. Those who bear the cross for their siblings and parents are loyal children, and those who bear the cross for the people of the kingdom are loyal subjects and virtuous women. When we possess the love of the Father, we become loyal children, and when we possess the love of the king, we become loyal subjects and virtuous women.

Today, how much have you developed the path of the cross that must overcome the era's environment? Are you not walking the path of the personal cross? With that alone, you cannot live for God. You must not be someone who places the cross on God as you move from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and global stage. You must stand and bear God's cross, crying out to God as a loyal child and a loyal subject, proclaiming that my blood and flesh cannot be united with the evil blood and flesh. Only then can the kingdom establish a relationship with you, and the Father can establish a direct relationship with you.

You must clearly understand this and become a group that fulfills its responsibilities as the vanguard on the path of the cross. Now the teacher is gathering blessed families to embark on a new adventure.

Tonight, go back and think about what stage you are in. Do you wish for the fulfillment of the will? Who will fulfill this will? Who, who will fulfill it? Can God do it alone? Humans must match the pace on the ground.

You have a path to walk, so you must tighten your belts. You must not be careless. It is a busy walk. Do not become a dropout on the path you must run, and I ask that you become those who can serve the Father in the promised unity and achieve victory in the Father's kingdom. Do you understand? Raise your hand if you are willing to do that.

Only those who have the conviction to win personal battles for the sake of their families can receive personal blessings, and only those who have the conviction to win battles for their families, tribes, nations, and the world can receive national blessings. We can understand that there are such principles through historical facts. 

So, what should Christians facing the end times do? They must not be tainted by the evil world but rather dominate it. No matter how great the pain, suffering, and misery they encounter in reality, and no matter how many unjust and resentful facts there may be, they must protect themselves from these. Those who cannot do this cannot manage the present age and will not be able to receive blessings in the new age that is to come. 

Therefore, Christians around the world today, who are facing the end, must not only manage their own lives but also manage their families, tribes, nations, and strive to overcome the global trials with a conviction to do so. If everyone does not unite with such conviction and take responsibility for their living and environmental stages, God cannot give them the blessings He wants to bestow. 

So, what is God looking for in today’s world? He is looking for a church that can emerge as a global religion among the many Christian churches scattered around the world. He will also seek families that can emerge as global families. In other words, He is looking for individuals, families, tribes, nations that can judge and settle everything beyond the path of suffering and the cross of reality. You must understand this well. 

If such a nation were to emerge, what kind of traditional aspects should its people possess? Whether they are the highest or the lowest in that nation, all must be able to overcome even if they find themselves in the worst positions in this world. Today, we must be able to judge this world and build a new ideological world, a heavenly kingdom. God does not bless those who cannot do this. Do you understand? 

God wants to raise us as victorious sons and daughters, giving us blessings on personal, familial, tribal, national, and global levels. While God has promised to give, there has been no individual, family, tribe, nation, or country in history that has realized that promise and laid the foundation for victory. What God longs for is to quickly share global blessings with all people through the ideology of such a nation. This is the heartfelt sentiment of God, who has been providentially working for 6,000 years without rest, and we must understand this today. 

God's urgent heart toward this world 
At one time, God, who was beyond the cosmic accusations, said, "You are my sons and daughters whom I can love eternally, and all this is yours. This entire creation, prepared for you through the past, present, and future, is for you to enjoy happiness for eternity." He has blessed individuals, families, tribes, and nations. By doing so, if you achieve victory personally, you will receive personal blessings at some point, and if you achieve victory as a family, you will receive family blessings at some point.

The need for individuals is to find families; the need for families is to find tribes; the need for tribes is to find nations; the need for nations is to find the world. Therefore, before seeking the world, you must first achieve victory on a national level. No matter how many victorious generals there may be in a country, if they lose in the final battle that determines the fate of that nation, they will become losers.

In the end, the issue here is conviction. There is nothing else. Without conviction, you will fail in the global battle. Even if you fall, you must say that you will do your best for this nation and the world before you fall. However, such a person has not yet appeared. You must have the determination to seek the global stage.

Value is determined by purpose.

God has been calling out for 6,000 years with open arms. Where are my beloved sons and daughters? Where is the family that must be fulfilled with blessings? Where are the tribes, the nation, and the sovereign, or the world?

For not just a day but for 6,000 years, He has been searching. He is our Father, who has been searching in such a miserable way. The Father is immersed in sorrow, shedding tears and lamenting. If you look at this image of the Father, you must forget various places and environments and have a sincere heart that knows how to struggle to not miss that voice, whether you live or die. Only then will the path be bright.

The teacher has fought to open this path until now. However, since there is still a path to walk, the teacher cannot be discouraged or tired here. When going toward the world based on Korea, even if you do not fulfill your responsibilities, the teacher must take responsibility.

The teacher longs for the unified group that can be proud and blessed for eternity. He also hopes that this nation will receive the blessings that all people can receive, and he looks forward to the day when the sovereign of this nation can receive the blessings that all sovereigns can receive. This is the path that a filial child serving God must take, and it is the duty that a loyal subject and virtuous woman must establish. Thinking of these things, we must fulfill our responsibilities until the end. So, we should be able to say, "May the joy and rewards of tomorrow that will come to us be given to all people." We must also be able to say, "May what I have received remain as the property of all people."

To give precious and blessed things to all people, God has carried personal crosses, family crosses, and countless historical crosses until now. Knowing this, if the teacher has received blessings, it would be unbearable not to give those blessings to all people. If I do not evangelize for even a day, I cannot live. You must either think for the nation or think of public matters and live; you must not live centered on yourself.

Value is determined by purpose. Why were we born, why do we live, and why do we die? It is not to become the wife of a certain husband or the husband of a certain wife. We were born for one purpose. Whether one becomes a wife or a husband, the purpose must be one. The values must be the same for the purpose to be the same. Therefore, husbands and wives must be ideal partners united by the same values. Such families and households must exist for the sake of the nation and the state.

You have inherited the tradition that God wants to give. Given that you are such people, when will you personally give to the thirty million people? When will you give for the 3 billion people of humanity? You cannot imagine how much God is longing for that day. When have you ever tried to give for the thirty million people or the 3 billion people? Have you ever given for heaven and earth or for God? You have struggled and lamented wanting to give, but you have neither given nor received.

God does not abandon those who take responsibility.

With such a heartfelt desire to give and receive, preparing to stand in a great position while practicing the way of loyalty to God requires much time and effort. Not only that, but sacrifices must follow. You must clearly understand that everything God wants to give is supported in proportion to that effort and sacrifice.

Among you gathered here today, how many will remain in a few years? Many people have followed the path the teacher has walked until now and then left. Nevertheless, the teacher continues. External trials have come, human trials have come, and personal desires have come, but the teacher has not been captured and made a prisoner by them. So, they have all passed.

Will the teacher be occupied by national trials like those of the Republic of Korea? No, that is not the case. According to God's wishes, following the will that God has left behind, my body and heart are running toward the place where God can dwell.
I'm going. If there are those among you who are unable to do so right now, you must at least prepare to comfort God in this historically sad place and struggle to fulfill this responsibility until I die. At such times, God can bless you, saying, "Even if this land of Korea is cursed and doomed, it is your land, the place where you shed tears..." This is how a nation can survive, and humanity can endure.

If there are individuals who establish a victorious foundation through the connection of human hearts to God's heart, that individual will be revered by all people, and if there are such families, nations, and states, they will be honored by all nations of the world. When that happens, a global center will be established, and only then will the world be properly positioned and function as it should.

So what is the path we are taking? We are currently working. When we think about the task of organizing Abel on God's side, this is an enormous fact. When this grows, this country will survive, and this world will survive. Considering this point, we must do anything here with enthusiasm.

Therefore, you should not make God, who has come with the desire to give, feel disappointed and send Him back, but rather comfort Him. You must allow Him to feel at ease because of you. Although the command is ten, if you act and take responsibility as if it were fifteen, then God will take responsibility for the remaining five. You must understand that God is with such people.

If our Unification Church says that it will take responsibility for what this thirty million nation cannot do, God will not abandon us. The teacher knows well that heaven shows compassion in proportion to the responsibility we take on.

Blessings received must be returned to all people
When you receive the blessings that God wants to give, you must return them to all people. However, from now on, do not share the blessings you have received. If you share the blessings before paving the way, you will not be able to pave the way. You must clearly understand the reason why you cannot share blessings right now. Do you understand what I mean?

Jesus also came to the foundation that God had prepared for 4,000 years to share blessings. This foundation connects all historical backgrounds of 6,000 years and all emotional connections.

Now that the foundation for sharing has been prepared, you, who must appear as representatives to share, must not defile this historical foundation. You must prepare to share. During this preparation period, you must become those who can receive well and return well, so that you can stand in a glorious position to share blessings in the future era. In other words, you will become true filial sons and daughters. Do you understand what I mean?

In your hearts, you should hope for the inheritance of hope and be able to act in a way that gives. You must give for individuals through families, and for families, you must give for whatever aspect, region, or community. It is a principle to give for your hometown and your parents and to receive honor from there.

Many people have come throughout history, but they have all passed. However, I hope that you will fulfill this solemn responsibility and remain as the victorious sons and daughters of God, as a channel to share blessings with all humanity. Do you understand? If you are willing to do so, please raise your hand.

There are countless warriors of unification scattered across the world. The path that true parents and true children must take
As you all know, today is the fifth Parents' Day we are celebrating. The ideology of Parents' Day was originally the central ideology within God's creation ideology. After God created all things, He created humans to govern those things and blessed them to govern all things for the purpose of establishing true parents.

The relationship between Parents' Day and God's providence
Originally, Adam and Eve were to become true parents centered on God. Then, Parents' Day would be established. When that happens, the entire universe would sing praises in the name of parents. Thus, Parents' Day is a day of joy when the entire universe sings praises in the name of parents.

It was God's wish to celebrate this day. However, due to the fall of the human ancestors, both heaven and earth lost this Parents' Day. Therefore, God has been working to fulfill what was originally planned and to find Parents' Day until now.

April 12, 1964, Daegu Church.
* This message was given on the occasion of the fifth Parents' Day during the third Principle Lecture Conference, and the title was added by the editor.

To celebrate Parents' Day, we must first welcome true parents. These true parents must be central beings who will judge history, govern the present, and pioneer the future. Therefore, what humanity has historically longed for has been to welcome true parents.

Who are the true parents who must appear on this earth on behalf of God's will? They must fight against the satanic world on behalf of all things, establish a position to govern all things, destroy the satan who governs the human world on behalf of humanity, and establish an absolute position that can govern countless spirits in the spiritual realm. True parents have such a mission. Therefore, God has paved the way until now to send true parents to restore the fallen world, to restore a world connected from all things to humans and heaven.

We have learned through the principle of restoration that for true parents to appear, there must be true sons and daughters, and for true sons and daughters to appear, there must be true servants. Looking at the history of God's restoration, we can see that God has worked through the age of servants, the age of children, and now to celebrate Parents' Day. We have also learned through the principle that spirits in the spiritual realm have cooperated throughout the process from the age of servants to the age of adopted children and the age of children to the age of parents.

Before true parents can come to this earth, a global foundation must be established beyond the standards of an individual nation. Therefore, after a period of 2,000 years of providential history passing through Noah and Abraham, God allowed Jacob to finally lay the foundation to form the Israelite nation. And He allowed that nation to form a state. It has taken countless historical processes to reach that point.

To achieve this, individuals must overcome Satan on God's behalf, adopted children must fight and win against Satan on God's behalf, and direct sons and daughters must also fight and win against the satanic world on God's behalf. Otherwise, true parents cannot be welcomed. That is why the providential history has been unfolding from the Old Testament era through the New Testament era until now.

Thus, after restoring the position of servants and the position of adopted children, God aimed to establish the relationship of true parents by restoring the position of direct sons and daughters, that is, after laying the foundation of victory, God sent the Messiah to this earth.

The purpose of God sending the Messiah
Due to the disbelief of the Israelite nation, the foundation of servants that God had prepared for 4,000 years was destroyed, and the foundation of adopted children was also destroyed. Therefore, Jesus, who came 2,000 years ago, had to fight and win from the position of a servant, fight and win from the position of an adopted child, and then advance to the position of a direct son. We know that this was the position of Jesus.

After passing through the positions of adopted child and direct son, the purpose of God sending Jesus was to establish the relationship of true parents based on the Israelite nation. That was also the mission that Jesus had to fulfill on this earth. However, because Jesus was crucified, He could not lay the foundation of victory on a universal standard, and He has been pioneering the relationship of true parents centered on the spiritual realm.

However, He has not yet established personal, familial, national, or state positions. We understand that we have come this far by establishing individuals, families, nations, and states that respond to heaven's will.

In this global era, heaven will surely send the Lord, who is the bridegroom, as promised, at the end of time. Thus, He will choose a bride and lay the foundation of true victory. The position of true parents is the original position of the purpose of creation, and to establish such a position, God has fought for 6,000 years.

Therefore, it is not an exaggeration to say that the 6,000 years of restoration providence is a history aimed at finding true parents. These true parents represent the entire history of God's 6,000 years of providence. Thus, we must understand that the failure to find true parents represents the sorrow, pain, and grief of all humanity.

Human history can be said to be the history of restoring true parents. Without restoring true parents, there can be no true children, and before establishing the relationship of true children, there can be no true families, true tribes, true nations, states, worlds, or heaven. God has worked for 6,000 long years to establish this standard.

Jesus, who came 2,000 years ago, was the first to come to this earth in the glory of true parents. However, for Jesus to appear as true parents, that is, since true parents are the historical embodiment, Jesus could not simply achieve one-sided victory. He could not fulfill only the mission of a son; He had to fulfill the mission of a parent.

Jesus had to go through the process of restoring the position of a son in the physical realm and the process of restoring the position of a parent in the spiritual realm. He had to fulfill responsibilities from both sides to establish a point of unity with God. Only then could that point become the foundation of individual Israel, the foundation of familial Israel, the foundation of national Israel, and the foundation of state Israel. If this had happened, the standard of true parents could have been established spiritually and physically, but due to the disbelief of the Israelite nation, that standard could not be established.

The returning Lord must inherit the spiritual foundation of Jesus
Originally, true parents, according to the principle of creation, must be those who have received God's blessings spiritually and physically. However, due to the disbelief of the Israelite nation, Jesus could not become true parents. Jesus also paved the way in the spiritual realm to establish a foundation to welcome true parents.

What does this mean? The Lord who is to return to this earth must restore the position of spiritual parents and the position of physical parents. Knowing this, Jesus has been in the spiritual realm for 2,000 years, doing what?
The Lord who is to come again has laid the foundation so that He will not be persecuted or violated by the spiritual world. He has established a spiritual society, nation, and global foundation centered on Jesus. 

Because Jesus has been governing not on earth but in the spiritual world, all those who believe in Christianity have formed a connection with spiritual parents. The Lord who returns to this earth must inherit the spiritual foundation that Jesus has established in the spiritual world, just as Jesus inherited all blessings from John the Baptist. Without going through such a position, it is impossible to establish a connection with the True Parents on this earth.

It is a principle to set the standard for spiritual inheritance on earth. This means that when Christians on earth inherit the spiritual foundation from the Lord who is to come again, they can unite, and the standard of inheritance can be established on earth. However, until now, Christians have not been able to set such a standard, and as a result, the foundation of spiritual victory has not been fully transferred to the True Parents who are coming again. Therefore, the returning True Parents must restore the standard of spiritual inheritance and go through a historical struggle to restore the standard of physical inheritance.

Originally, God has been governing for 6,000 years to prepare the foundation for the coming True Parents and to establish a victorious foundation in that era. However, because the saints on this earth have not united and followed the commands of their spiritual parents, they have not been able to set the standard for inheriting the spiritual foundation that Jesus has established until now.

Thus, the Lord who is to come again, who will become the True Parents, must undergo personal trials in the spiritual world, as well as trials on the family, tribe, nation, and global levels. Without overcoming those trials and establishing the standard of internal victory, it is impossible to establish the standard of substantial victory on earth, and thus, internal struggles cannot be avoided.

So what is the Principle of Restoration? It is the principle that enables victory in the spiritual battle, that is, overcoming the internal cross. It is also the principle that can restore all the sad events that have historically occurred. By establishing a substantial entity on earth that connects the victory in the spiritual realm to the earth, we can finally restart the global Canaan restoration path that Jesus intended to begin 2,000 years ago.

We must develop the battle in the spiritual world and the substantial world centered on the coming True Parents, but such battles have not yet been fully engaged on earth.

Trials the Coming True Parents Must Endure
There must be two True Parents. Without two, one cannot stand on the foundation of True Parents. Even if the standard of victory is established in the spiritual battle, if the substantial True Parents are not established on earth, the standard of victory in the substantial world cannot be established. No matter how many conditions of victory are achieved in the spiritual world, if the True Parents are not established on earth, the foundation corresponding to that spiritual world cannot be laid on this earth.

For this reason, the True Parents who are to come must dedicate their lives to fight on behalf of heaven and earth. We must understand that this period of struggle lasts for 40 years. 

What kind of battles must the coming True Parents go through during this 40-year period? First, they must undergo spiritual trials in the spiritual world. Next, they must face substantial trials on earth. Even amidst these, they must maintain their center without falling, and only then can they establish the connection of True Parents in unity of spirit and body. In other words, they can fulfill the hope of 6,000 years of providential history.

In 1960, we established Parents' Day. What kind of day is that? It is the day when the point of true victory was established through the unity of spirit and body, and it is the day when the ideology of True Parents began. Therefore, that day is not just a single day; the connection of that day, although it may seem partial, will go through a universal connection.

And God was able to simultaneously implement plans in the spiritual and physical realms starting from that day. In other words, the foundation that can resonate with the spiritual world has finally been laid, allowing God to fight.

Because the foundation of victory has been established, it is sufficient to lay the family foundation, tribal foundation, national foundation, and global foundation that align with it.

Just as Jesus could not complete his overall mission due to the opposition of the Israelite people and went to paradise to spiritually restore Israel, standing in the position of spiritual parents, the time when the global victory can be established on earth is the four-year course.

During this four-year course, when the spiritual and physical realms unite to establish the point of victory, the entire world will enter an era of benefits where humanity can march into the spiritual world beyond paradise.

However, in going through this historical process, the coming True Parents must bear the cross of the individual at the stage of personal trials, bear the cross of the family at the stage of familial trials, and bear the cross of the tribe, nation, and world at the respective stages.

Significance of the 3-Year, 4-Year, and 40-Year Courses
Looking at the history of the Israelite people, Jacob was able to set the condition for personal restoration because he won in his personal struggle with Esau. After that, he went to Laban's house and was able to find his family because he won in the familial battle with heaven's cooperation. Later, Jacob's descendants entered Egypt, the world of Satan, to form a nation, and they were rescued with heaven's cooperation and were able to enter Canaan and defeat the seven nations of Canaan. Thus, the Israelite people were finally able to attack the world of Satan after going through the 40-year course of Canaan restoration.

Before the 40-year wilderness course, there was a 3-day course. The Israelite people could only return to Canaan after going through the 3-day course. And once they entered Canaan, they had to establish another 40 years.

Because the restoration providence has gone through such courses, until now, the teacher has also had to go through the 40-year course, and then the 3-year course and the 4-year course. Therefore, we have walked the 3-year course and are now walking the 4-year course. Adding the 3-year course and the 4-year course gives us the 7-year course.

Through this process, we can finally conclude the history of restoration and establish the sovereignty of heaven. Jesus originally had to walk a 7-year course from the age of 33 to establish the standard of parents that God desires, and from there, establish the standard for the restoration of all things by the age of 40, concluding everything and fulfilling heaven's will. This was Jesus' mission, but because he could not fulfill this will and died on the cross, this will remained unfulfilled.

Thus, the returning True Parents cannot avoid taking responsibility for internal and external battles, going through a 40-year preparation period or struggle period. Externally, that 40-year period is a preparation period, but internally, it is a period of struggle. In this way, by establishing a foundation of victory spiritually, they can finally lay the substantial foundation of unity of spirit and body on earth.

The True Parents must go through the 3-year course centered on themselves and the 4-year course to prepare for the restoration of all things, that is, to establish the foundation for the four directions. Thus, they must conclude the restoration of indemnity through the 7-year course.

Looking at the historical course until finding the True Parents, the 3-year course, 4-year course, and 40-year course are short courses, but they are the periods for restoring all historical sadness, for restoring all historical divisions, and for restoring all historical crosses. Without establishing an absolute standard that does not succumb to all historical sadness, pain, and division, we cannot meet the Day of True Parents and the Day of True Parents' Victory.

On behalf of heaven, on behalf of the connection with True Parents, our Unification Church is therefore undergoing such trials. In the process, we must establish ourselves as distinct from the world of Satan and set the standard of true children who can take the example of True Parents' victory to judge the world of Satan. Without establishing the standards of tribe, nation, and country, we cannot fulfill the original will of True Parents on this earth.

During this period, you who are fighting alongside me are personal representatives, familial representatives, tribal representatives, and national representatives of True Parents. As such representatives of parents, you have been fighting in various regions of South Korea until now. Now, it is your responsibility to go out and fight on the global stage.

From this perspective, what has been the sadness of the spiritual and physical worlds until now? Originally, when the True Parents appear on this earth, from that day on, heaven and earth should sing of peace, and the entire universe should enter into the realm of happiness, and the heavenly kingdom on earth should be established centered on God. However, the earth we live on is not a kingdom.

We are still on the path toward the kingdom. We are progressing toward the world through the individual, family, tribe, and nation. Now, we have passed the 40-year course and the 3-year course, and we are walking the 4-year course to face the seven nations of Canaan. The issue here is how to restore the Korean people, who represent the seven nations of Canaan. You must clearly understand this.

Difficulties of Restoring Parents
You who are centered on the restoration of Korea are individuals, but you must understand that you are not just walking your own path. You must remember that you are going as representatives of True Parents. Without this understanding, you cannot prepare the foundation for the victory of the tribal, national, or parental level.

To properly go as representatives of True Parents, if True Parents are going out to establish the standard of global spiritual victory, you must go out to establish the standard of national victory. Spiritually, the standard of victory for True Parents has been established, so we must establish the standard of victory for True Parents on earth, and you are fulfilling the responsibility of True Parents that must go beyond the national standard.

To explain this from another perspective, if you are moving toward a global standard beyond the national standard, the returning True Parents must establish the standard of victory that is universal. The Lord who comes with the connection of True Parents must spiritually pioneer the cross we must bear, achieve substantial victory, and take responsibility for everything. This is the difficulty of restoring parents that you must understand.

Now, when we look at heaven, earth, and humanity today, when has heaven had the victorious True Parents? Heaven has not yet had them. Has the earth had them? The earth has not yet had them. Have humans had them? Humans have not yet had them. We are still on that path.

So, is it enough to just have True Parents? No, it is not. After having True Parents, we must restore true families, tribes, nations, and the world. The people prepared for this were the Israelite people.

To stand as true children before True Parents, there must be a personal restoration course for the children, a familial restoration course for the children, a tribal restoration course for the children, a national restoration course for the children, and a global restoration course for the children. The restoration courses of the parents at the personal, family, tribe, nation, and global levels and the restoration courses of the children at the personal, family, tribe, nation, and global levels must be completed, and only after establishing the standard of victory where parents and children are one can we conclude the restoration of the nation and newly start toward the global stage.

Looking at the 6,000 years of heaven's restoration history, the 6,000 years of restoration history is both a history of restoring parents and a history of restoring children. Therefore, if the parents have built a foundation of personal victory, the children must also build a foundation of personal victory by following that victory. If the parents have created a foundation of familial victory, the children must also create a foundation of familial victory by following that victory.

If the parents have established a foundation of victory at the personal, family, tribe, nation, and global levels, the children must also establish a foundation of victory at the personal, family, tribe, nation, and global levels. Only when the foundation of victory of the parents and the foundation of victory of the children are in alignment can we establish the standard of national victory and the standard of national restoration.

What standard did we establish as we walked the 3-year course? Did we not say to walk the path of restoration with the heart of parents, using the bodies of servants, shedding blood, sweat, and tears? Therefore, while you stand in the position of children, you must go with the heart of parents.

When we look at the Unification Church centered on the ideology of parents, the blessed families are forming the tribes of heaven, and the entire members centered on blessed families are forming the nation of heaven. In this way, we are addressing this 30 million nation. This includes not only the national standard but also the tribal standard, family standard, and individual standard. Such tribal standards are being developed from a horizontal perspective.

However, looking at you now, you still seem to be in the state of the initial start, and the way you are currently active is also the same as at the beginning.

Mission of the Unification Church
You may be individuals who have not yet established a proper foundation of victory, but through the connection with True Parents, if you establish conditions aligned with True Parents, you can lay the foundations of personal victory, familial victory, tribal victory, national victory, and global victory. That period is the 7-year course. Therefore, if you establish the standard of national victory centered on the connection with True Parents, only then can God begin to govern all things. Furthermore, He can govern all things, establish the heavenly family, and establish an unshakeable sovereignty on heaven and earth, a single people, and a single territory. From that point, God can rest eternally, and judgment will begin from there.

When we look at Jesus, he was sent based on one nation and one people. However, did the Israelite people, who were to be the foundation for that, who God had worked for 4,000 years to establish as the foundation of personal, familial, tribal, national victory, stand in the position to welcome Jesus? The Israelite people could not do so.

The Lord who is to come is the center representing the spiritual and substantial worlds, so the Israelite people had to unite with the Lord. Only when the Israelite people were united with the Lord could they establish the foundations of personal, familial, tribal, national victory and find the connection with True Parents, thus being able to make a global start. However, the Israelite people could not unite with Jesus and disbelieved him. Therefore, Jesus had no choice but to die on the cross.

So what is the mission of the Unification Church today, and what position do you who have joined the Unification Church stand in? You who have been called to this Unification Church centered on the teacher are in the position to unfold the sorrowful 6,000-year vertical history horizontally and substantially.

What resolution must we make now? What is our goal? We must establish the nation of True Parents on a global foundation. We must establish the nation of True Parents on a global scale. There is still sadness, pain, and tears remaining in this world, and we must resolve these as soon as possible. This is the responsibility and mission that the Unification Church must undertake today.
Therefore, you have now embarked on the path you must take, and just like the Israelites who were heading toward Canaan, you must not look back. This must be true in both heart and body.

True devotion to True Parents
Now, what is the hope we must embrace? We must sincerely hope to serve True Parents who come to this earth on behalf of Heaven. We should not expect to serve them in a place where victory has been established, where all people look up to and respect them. We must hope to serve True Parents as they go through a sorrowful history.

The ancestors regarded the inability to serve True Parents, who are going through a sorrowful history, as a deep sorrow. To truly serve True Parents is the hope of all humanity. That is why Jesus said, "Come to me, all you who are weary and burdened, and I will give you rest." (Matthew 11:28) However, we must also be able to say, "My yoke is easy and my burden is light." 

To fulfill a responsibility that is three times greater, the earnest desire to give love is God's heart and the heart of a true parent. When a parent sees the burden that their children bear, the heavier that burden is, and the more miserable they are, the more the desire to give arises in proportion to that misery, and the more earnest that heart becomes. Because God is such a being, although He is in a position to receive, His desire to give is greater, and because of that compassionate heart, the power of greater love bursts forth. That is why God has been able to endure this pain until today while carrying an infinite burden. 

You will have to take on responsibilities that are three times greater in the future, but how should you walk this path? This path cannot be walked by focusing on your own circumstances. So, what position should you take? You must not think that you are more miserable and pitiful than those who do not know their own path. Do not view yourself through the standards of those people. You must think that you are bearing a responsibility that is three times greater than anyone else walking any other path of virtue. This applies to other members of the Unification Church as well. Those who go ahead first must be recognized as those who are preparing for the future. There will be those who must walk this path to lay the foundation for the restoration through indemnity. 

When you see it this way, you must not stand in a position where you compare yourself to others, saying, "I am miserable, but they are not," or "They are miserable, but I am not." 

So how should you overcome these difficult trials? When God sees the poor humans in the position of His children carrying a great cross and standing in a path of great suffering, even if they are descendants of the fallen, God is principled and carries absolute responsibility. Because He has a heart full of love that wants to give, He does not reduce His love just because they are suffering. The heart of a fallen world's parent is like that, but the original heart of God is even greater. 

The more miserable they are, the more earnest the desire to give becomes. Because God, who has this heart of love and desire to give, has walked the path of suffering for 6,000 years, carrying a heavy burden, He does not have the recognition that He has done well and fulfilled His responsibility. You must be the same. However, because you are trying to receive and are centered on yourself in forming connections, you feel exhausted and overwhelmed. 

How did it come to be that humans, who should receive God's love and enjoy blessings and happiness, ended up like this? True Understanding of God 
We have lived until now in a fallen world. I am a being existing in a fallen world. Our family is also a family in a fallen world. That is why I must long for living in the homeland, serving my parents in the homeland, and living with my siblings in the homeland. I should be serving my father in the homeland, but how should I serve Him? Should I serve Him as a widower? Should I serve Him in the miserable environment I have lived in until now? Should I serve Him in a position of receiving service, or in a position of serving Him? In what position should I serve Him? I must not serve Him from a position of receiving service. 

Internally, I must offer all service to God, and in an ideological sense, God serves us. If I properly manage everything internally and return it well to God, then God will come to us. 

To allow God to come to us in a familial way, I must manage myself. I must manage individuals according to that ideology, manage families according to that ideology, and manage tribes, nations, and countries according to that ideology. If I do not do that, it will be impossible. 

Today, the Unification Church calls each other family. While you call each other family, you must understand that the current positions you are in do not provide a foundation to live as a family. We must seek the homeland and the homeland's nation and world. And what will we do there? We must become filial sons and daughters and loyal subjects and virtuous women. No matter how much we are serving and being loyal now, we must not fail to attain the status of filial sons and daughters and loyal subjects and virtuous women when we get there. 

Therefore, we must say, "Farewell, world. I am going. Hurry up, time. Hurry up, long and arduous path of suffering." The suffering that comes to my individual is only temporary. And to you, Satan, who raises the flag of enmity! When the trials that come to my family pass, you will be the last. To you, Satan, who brings trials to our tribe! When the trials you give pass through our tribe, you will be the last. 

You must be able to say this. All the suffering from Satan that comes to our nation and country will also be the last when it passes through us. No matter how fierce the suffering is and how miserable the facts are, we must have the conviction that it is the last. 

I must put a final point on the hope that I, my family, my tribe, my nation, and the world desire. And after it becomes the last, what will we do? We will rejoice and enjoy. We will enter the new heaven and earth and establish a heavenly kingdom on earth to live with countless humanity.
