God's Hardships in the Restoration Providence 
When God raises historical figures like Noah or Abraham, the earnest heart He has is beyond words. When He raises that one person, He does not do so merely to represent a nation. He raises them as someone responsible for the restoration of the world. In this way, God chooses and raises individuals from a historical, temporal, future, and even a global perspective. However, if that chosen person makes a mistake, the foundation for the global restoration is lost. 

In such a case, God must choose a successor to indemnify the mistakes made by the previous person and hand it over to that person. This is the condition of sorrow that God carries when choosing a person. For this reason, we must understand that every time God chooses a person, He experiences infinite internal pain and external hardships. 

When we look at the Bible, it says not to make oaths. Why did it say not to make oaths? Why has God not taught and guided humanity about the certain limits they can be responsible for? You must understand the sorrowful heart of God who cannot teach. 

When someone swears, "I will take on this responsibility. I will fulfill this responsibility at some point," if that person fails, their failure is linked to God's failure. Moreover, the failure of that person’s descendants is connected to the failure of humanity today and the failure of the purpose of history. 

That is why God is in a position to require oaths from humans today, but He cannot receive them. He is in a position to teach and advise everything, but He cannot do so. How great must God's anguish be? You must understand this. 

Even in such a position, God wants to do more for those who are loyal to His will than anything else in the world. He wants to boast about them more than anything else in the world and has the desire to give everything in heaven and earth to them, but He cannot do so. Why? Because when He chooses a loyal person and raises them, they must completely establish any standard He intends, and because the gifts that God gives are global gifts, even if that person is loyal, God cannot give until that standard is fully achieved, even if He has the desire to give. 

We must serve God, who comes forth with such a heart of longing, and we must understand that He is the God who treats us with such a heart of longing. 

So, how will we meet God today? This is the question. In what position will we meet Him? Most people will want to meet Him in a blessed position filled with joy, embracing heaven and earth and commanding the universe. This has been the general desire and hope of all humanity until now. However, you cannot meet God in such a position. 

The True Place to Meet God 
For example, let’s say a father is building a great house. This father does not have a lot of money, nor does he have all the necessary materials, but after great effort, he builds a house that everyone envies. On a joyful day, he will reflect on his past and think about the hardships he endured. The greater that hardship, the greater the joy of that day will be in proportion. However, the children in the position of sons will think about how their father suffered when he was building the house.
I could not come to you, not knowing my father's circumstances, and kept my distance from him. 
Let us say that such sons have come to visit their father, who is celebrating a joyful day, to share in that joy. How would the father have treated them at that moment? 
Would he say, "You are my beloved sons, let us share in this joy together"? Rather, seeing the faces of those sons would remind him of the sad past. Even if those sons regret not having supported their father, we can understand that it would only bring pain and sadness to a day of joy. 
Just like this father, God has suffered infinitely and faced countless hardships while coming forth to fulfill the purpose of the overall restoration. However, countless humans in the position of children have not cooperated with God. God, who has overcome each difficult hill of the cross, hoped that humans would cooperate. He needed companions. 
Without companions, God cannot overcome those hills. Even personal hills of the cross cannot be overcome without human support. Likewise, when overcoming the hills of the family, nation, or world, without companions, He cannot succeed. If there is no substantial offering that is wholeheartedly dedicated to establishing loyalty before God, who bears the responsibility of the world’s cross, then God cannot overcome this hill either. 
We must understand that God has been longing for sons and daughters who can accompany Him on this path of restoration. 
In any case, the purpose of restoration will be concluded, and God's providential will shall be fulfilled. When that happens, a day will come when God can rejoice. What will God look like on that day? He will appear with a heart full of tears, having endured countless hardships, having crossed the hills of the cross thousands and millions of times, bearing a pitiful and miserable appearance. We must recognize that we arrive at that day through such a process. 
If you are to attend such a gathering, even if you cannot directly cooperate with God's work, you must be able to feel God's sorrowful heart, which has labored solely to prepare this one day for the liberation of all humanity and for a happy life. 
You must have a heart that can repent and weep before God, who has arrived at the day of joy. 
You should reflect on why you did not know your father, and why you did not understand the position that your father was worried about. You must repent and feel indignant. 
If you have such a reflective heart regarding your past life, there is room for God to sympathize with you. It is not acceptable to simply participate without such a heart. It is not everyone who says to me, "Lord, Lord," who will enter the kingdom of heaven, but only those who do the will of my Father in heaven. (Matthew 7:21) This is the reason why this statement is in the Bible. 
We are on our way to meet God. It is the desire of every person to meet the joyful God, but we must never forget that until God appears as the joyful God, He walks through sorrow and all kinds of hardships. 
So, what kind of God have you been with while walking the path of the cross until now? You must be able to comfort God's loneliness by sharing in His sorrow when He is sad, weeping over His pitiful state, and vowing to take responsibility for the path of the cross that He has walked. If there are such sons and daughters, then when that joyful day comes, God will call them forth and present them before all creation, before the universe, wanting to establish that joyful day as the day of His children rather than His own. We must understand that this is God's heart. 
For this reason, God has sought such sons and daughters, and when we realize that He hopes for brothers, families, societies, nations, and the world made up of such sons and daughters, we must recognize how great our responsibility is as we stand on the path of restoration. 
If you wish to be someone who must carry God, you should want all of humanity to carry God and treat all of humanity as brothers. Thus, you must set a condition to be a model for them in carrying God, allowing them to comfort God, and have a heart to prevent God's sorrow. Such a person is a son or daughter of God. 
There is no greater reward, hope, praise, or happiness than meeting God. 
When I am sad, the place where God comes to meet me is infinitely happy. You must understand that the place where you go to meet God, who is suffering, is also infinitely happy. 
When Jesus was crucified, God came to that place, and the angels bowed their heads, participating in that sorrow. However, Jesus understood that in order to meet such a day, He had to overcome the inner pain of God's heart, and He realized that the sorrow of having to be sent to that place was great. That is why He prayed, "My Father... not as I will, but as You will." (Matthew 26:39) In this way, Jesus connected with God's inner heart and established the standard of that heart on this earth. 
Therefore, meeting God is not just about meeting Him in a joyful place. Meeting Him in a sorrowful place is the true meeting with God. We must stand in a position to historically comfort God in sorrow, to protect Him in reality, and to remove the environment of the cross on His behalf. This is the position that God, who is seeking His children, desires. It is what everyone wishes for, that after God has accomplished all things, He will call His sons and daughters to celebrate the joyful day. However, God wishes to meet us in a sorrowful place, even if all people do not desire that. 
Today, as you walk the path of restoration, you must always keep in mind that you are the one who will carry God. Regardless of how the world is, how your environment is, how your body is, or how your situation is, you must think, "I will carry God; carrying God is my destiny." 
There is no one on this earth who is striving with a desperate heart to resolve the grievances of our ancestors who betrayed God. That is why God holds on to humans who are becoming captives of Satan. He blocks the arrows of the enemy. You must be able to experience this reality. 
You should not rejoice just because you received some recognition during a church event. You should not be happy just because you received praise. You must understand that God's heart, which faces the countless people in heaven and earth, desires to bless everyone. You must think about how to pave the way for them to receive blessings. 
Even if there is something that can be praised, I do not wish to be praised. There is still a path of restoration that I must walk, so I must go. My wish is to see my father’s joyful face when the will is fulfilled. 
This is what you should say. 
There is no greater reward than seeing God, no greater hope, no greater praise, and no greater happiness. Only those who move forward in this way can be said to be true filial sons and daughters. That is why everything we do, walk, and fight is for the purpose of meeting God. Is there no sorrow on the path to comfort God's sorrowful position and remove all the paths of the cross before humanity? This is the path of historical restoration. You must long to meet God. What God desires and aims for is my desire and my aim, and the path that God wishes to walk is the path I must walk. 
The perspective God has towards humans 
You must feel the sorrowful heart of God and humanity being separated due to the fall of our ancestors, Adam and Eve, 6,000 years ago. When reflecting on the long history, we can see that humanity has groaned in sorrow. However, you must think that God, looking at humans who are committing sins under the dominion of Satan, is more sorrowful than humans themselves. 
How did our ancestors create such a sorrowful history! Who has mourned over the grievances and injustices of this history, and who has fought alongside this historical resentment? From the beginning, God and our good ancestors have fought against this resentment. I was born to pass down the tradition of God and our good ancestors, and I was born to convey that thought and ideology. Therefore, we must have a heart that longs for a new world. When we look at this miserable reality, we must think that the responsibility to pioneer this unhappy and miserable reality lies with God. This is the path of God. 
When you see sorrowful events, you must first feel God's heart, which is more sorrowful than the person who is suffering. When you go to evangelize a certain city, you should go with tears in your eyes, asking, "Where am I going, Father? Where am I going? Who will I meet today? Am I meeting with the enemy or with a monster, or am I meeting with someone whom God wishes to fight and subdue?" Father! Who am I? I will go forth through one. I will go as the son of the Father who is responsible for this city. I will go as a daughter. I will go as a worker of God. I will go to uphold the way of true life. 
This is the position you must stand in. You must pave the true path from this position. 
You must uproot the weeds of the satanic world. By establishing conditions for victory on this earth, you must become the people of heaven and offer up that achievement. Now is the time when you can say to God that you will dedicate this city entirely to Him. Therefore, you must have the heart to seek those who can become offerings representing this nation through my footsteps. God sees people from this perspective. Although it may seem insignificant and nothing, when viewed from the internal perspective that admires God's heart, what you do is solemn. 
Noah devoted himself to God for 120 years, whether others saw it or not. You must understand that what Noah did became the condition to turn the joy of the ages. Although he worked alone and sweated, from the perspective that the world of lamentation is yearning for a day of liberation, what he did was to appeal for unspeakable happiness. God comes to humans with a hopeful heart, asking them to prepare for a day of hope. 
Who are you going for on this path? You are going to meet God. So how should you go to meet God? You must start with God, walk with God, and live in a place where you want to carry Him. 
When have we ever met God, and when have we ever lived carrying Him? We have never lived carrying Him. However, God is not a God who has escaped from this world. He is working for the poor people in the world, for the countless children who are groaning in the arms of the enemy. In this world, which is like a place of death, God is fulfilling the mission of a pioneer for a day of joy. You must have the conviction that you live on this stage. Not only should you live with such conviction, but you must also have the heart to subdue the enemy and relieve God's grievances. Only those who live and fight with such a mindset can meet God and live carrying Him. 
The value of life becomes meaningful when God is with you. 
When you meet God after achieving some purpose through your hard work, at that moment, God becomes your legally recognized Father. Therefore, even if you are in a place of tears, you must live carrying God within the realm of life where He is present. You must work with God, fight with Him, and live with Him. 
God does not grieve over His own cross. He does not live for Himself. He lives for all people and for His children. Therefore, you should not grieve over your own cross, nor should you live for yourself. You must live for all people. 
That is why, in the process of following your will, you must not only think that it is happy and grateful when the way opens and the environment welcomes you. You must long for the time when you were before God, shedding tears and praying in a narrow and miserable place. Only then will God be with you. When you move forward in this way, the hand of salvation will appear, and the hand of the prophet will appear. This is the place where God is with you. 
Therefore, the period of working in such a place will remain in your life. 
I believe in God. I remember the time when I appealed to God, swearing that I would not go alone in any pitiful place. I will never perish. I remember the time when I swore before God and prayed with a sincere heart whenever I faced trials against the enemy, Satan. 
Despite these circumstances, God could not teach me, could not receive my oath, and only comforted me. How pitiful must God have been to have to do this? What kind of God is it who, even when a person betrays Him after being loyal, cannot say, "Why do you betray me, my child?" You must understand the sorrowful heart of such a God. Meeting this God, who has been so sorrowful, is precious, but to meet Him joyfully, we must become God's emotional companions on the path leading up to that meeting. This is the normal meeting. 
Today, we live directly with our Father, acting and fighting against Satan. We must feel that living in such a time and having such a bond is an infinite happiness. What we are doing now is a significant matter that can influence the pride of the nation. Today, this world is spiritually confused. We have received a tremendous benefit in this era to change such a world. 
You must feel the thrill of deciding and pioneering this path to create such a world, sweating and fighting. The teacher knows that you have gathered here to feel this. Ordinary people tend to run away when they become aware of the overall movement. They say that there is no support to protect them. 
You must have confidence that you will win in the final battle. 
In the satanic world, when you receive a recommendation to do something, there is a protector behind you.
Everything is taken care of, and all practical issues are also managed. However, that is what the people of the satanic world do. They say it is pitiful that we take on the path of suffering. God knows us well, but He cannot take responsibility behind the scenes. How painful and sorrowful must God's heart be in this situation? You must lead all the family members who are weary from difficulties and go forward, no matter what hardships you face. How great must God's sorrow be knowing your struggles? 

Let’s go and keep going. We must manage our own environment in this way. God desires such people. The stage for the final struggle, which has never been seen in history, is a solemn and serious place, and God guarantees its historical value. From that perspective, God is pushing us from behind to give us heaven and earth.

You and I are taking on responsibilities in the Unification Church in our respective fields. The teacher is responsible in his field, and you are responsible in yours. In terms of taking responsibility, you and the teacher are the same. However, there is a significant difference in the areas of daily life and the mission behind it. Similarly, the areas in which God is working through providence are also vastly different.

Everyone, God has not been defeated. God has not underestimated the struggle to subdue Satan. He continues to fight. Even if this nation does not fight, and humanity does not fight, this struggle cannot be stopped. Why? Because if God has established a standard for building families, He can establish countless family members globally on this earth, and if He has established tribes, He can establish nations. This is the principle of heaven, and as long as we establish one center, a way to survive will surely emerge.

When this one center thrives, it will flourish in the same way. We must establish such principled standards and expand from families to nations and the world. Therefore, we can proceed based on the principles of heaven from our families. If there is a plus (+), a minus (-) will automatically arise.

This is also true when it comes to dealing with the will today. The one who will strike the traditions of the satanic world with something more important, more thorough, and more complete is the teacher. A great history will be written with that. You must do this work together with me.

The suffering that humanity is experiencing today is the last in our era. We must say that we have confidence in winning this battle on the Korean Peninsula. Does everyone have that confidence? This battle, which we are engaging in with all our heart, is the ultimate fierce battle and the final showdown. Throughout history, there have been many rises and falls globally, but this battle we are fighting must be the last battle in history. It must be the end along with the sorrows of history.

Let us become loyal children who dedicate ourselves for the day of victory. The path of filial piety. The victory of the last battle to restore the sinful world will come to this earth, and you must go. The final crisis of fighting centered on God will come, and you must go. The final crisis of fighting for the tribe will come, and you must go. The final crisis of fighting for this nation will come, and you must go. How much regret would there be if you cannot participate in this battle? How much regret would there be if you cannot wave the flag of victory and dominate the world?

Therefore, what you should hope for in your hearts is to welcome the day of victory. To meet this day, you must fight. Victory does not come without a fight. You must go through the struggle of whether to live or die, whether to perish or survive.

In this practical path, what have you done to bear your personal cross? What have you done to bear your family cross? Do you know how many struggles God has gone through to cross this hill, how much He has grieved, how much He has yearned, and how much He has struggled? How can humanity not overcome such a hill in one generation? Centered on 6,000 years of history, our Unification Church must overcome this hill of sorrow in one generation. In the future, personal enemies will disappear historically, and enemies of families, tribes, and nations will also disappear historically.

From this perspective, you must fight alongside God in the position of serving Him. You have learned the principles until now, but you have not fulfilled your responsibilities. The principles are separate, and you are separate in your own ways.

Today, we are unfolding the holy task of raising the first flag of victory for this nation. Therefore, since I have offered my blood and flesh before God, I must advance with the conviction to conquer the enemy's stronghold for the day of glory.

For this work, even if it takes 10 years, 100 years, or even a lifetime, you must have the conviction to go. Now, how we fulfill our loyalty is the issue. Whether Daegu City receives or does not receive is not the issue. The issue is whether I have fulfilled my loyalty or not, not whether it receives or does not receive. Whether the number of church members increases or not is not the issue. The issue is how much our members have given. When giving, it must be given in a way that allows it to return.

You are people who know the will and have truly devoted yourselves over the past three years. You must have seen many people who have complained and despaired while working for God's will during these three years. However, if God dwells in their hearts, they will change. Their suffering and struggle against global hardships are for the day of victory.

You must live a life that values the desire to serve God and approach Him, which is the path of filial piety. Do you understand what I mean? Then let’s start anew from today, just like the beginning.

Awake and pray with a true heart. 

<Summary of the Message> The revival meeting this time is being held at great expense because of you. Therefore, you must return to your local areas and revive yourselves. The teacher only slept for four hours even while out hunting. We must show the external through the revival meeting. From tomorrow, for three days, do not sleep, and the district leader must lead the way in street evangelism to bring more people to attend.

Can we sleep on the battlefield? For three days, pray to establish a spiritual standard, and even if it rains, we must work diligently to restore Daegu City. Do not sleep; stay awake and pray.

The teacher plans to tour the regions this year. We must not be defeated externally. We must achieve our goals even if it means fasting. Everything that is not on God's side must be judged.

Korea is a miniature of the world, and the regional leader, as the head of the district, is in a position similar to that of the high priest. Therefore, you must pray with tears and a true heart, bearing the heart of a mother giving birth. You must know that I am positioned at the focal point where countless arrows of Satan are aimed and concentrate your mind to pray earnestly.

God desires a true heart, so you must pray with a true heart. 

April 18, 1964 (Saturday) 10:30 PM, Daegu Church. 

* This message was given during the 3rd Principle Workshop held for 18 days in Daegu and is compiled from what was published in <Gyeonggi Front> No. 7. The title was added by the editor.

Let us give the true things to everyone. 

<Summary of the Message> For Abel's will to be established, the restoration of the relationship between God, angels, and Abel must align. Even during the times of Noah and Abraham, God's will and their will were aligned in both action and personality, which is why judgment could occur. Jesus also appeared centered on God's will.

Today, the Unification Church is a substantial existence that God is looking for, positioned in a place where spirits, ancestors, and angels, as well as God, are watching, and also representing them all. You must know this and act with such conviction.

If you wish for cooperation from the spirit world and God, you must establish goodness with a historical heart. A holy person is one who prays for God, the earth, and humanity even in loneliness.

Offerings are the substantial reality of historical indemnity and have a public purpose. A nation is the embodiment of history and the fruits of ancestors. Even in lonely places, you must know that you are not alone and that God is present. The world of restoration is achieved only by giving. It cannot be achieved by receiving. Therefore, you must give true heart and words. Only those who receive God's approval can have their sins forgiven. It is more earnest to pray for the church than for established church members.

April 19, 1964 (Sunday) 9:30 AM, Daegu Church. 

* This message was given before the start of evangelism during the 3rd Principle Workshop held for 18 days in Daegu and is compiled from what was published in <Gyeonggi Front> No. 7. The title was added by the editor.

Let us give the true things to everyone. 

You have come from various places in South Korea, so the fate of Korea and the world depends on this. 

With thousands of saints and heaven watching, we must give the true things with a solemn sense of mission. 

History and ancestors do not wish for the tribes that should become comrades to become enemies. 

Those who shed true tears on behalf of the nation and God will not be judged. 

When you think about your four-year journey for the nation, consider what kind of heart Jacob, Abraham, Moses, or Jesus had while walking the path of providence, and how lonely Jesus must have felt when no one acknowledged his suffering.

Those who shed tears on behalf of history and God will never perish. That is why, even in lonely places, we must become those who advance centered on God, so that we can be guaranteed by Him.

God establishes individuals to find nations, establishes nations to find states, and further seeks to find the world and heaven. 

You must elevate your hearts even more and become those who give true things with a loving heart to everyone.
